eva sanniveśaḥ pradeśeṣu mantavyaḥ, yathā-citrābhinayādāvarthaprakaraṇādivaśāttvanyatrāpi pravartyeta ।
yathā-- svastikavicyutikaraṇādityādau (9-21) patākayoge'pi tathāpi maṇibandhanavinyastatvaṃ
nāmānuyāyyeva rūpam । ata eva kecidetāvatāsya lakṣaṇaṃ pariśiṣṭaṃ tūdāharaṇadigarthamiti
pratipannāḥ । <q>strīprayojitā</q>viti । patākasvastikakarmāṇi strībhiramunaiva kāryāṇītyarthaḥ ।
svastikārthalakṣaṇasamākṛtitvātsvastikaḥ ।</p>
<p>khaṭakāvardhamānamāha <q>khaṭaka</q> iti labhyate । anye tvanyonyābhimukhaṃ khaṭakadvayamasya
rūpamityāhuḥ । khaṭakasya ā samantāt bahiryogādidaṃ nāma । śṛṅgārārtheṣu śṛṅgāraprayojaneṣu ।
tāmbūlagrahaṇādiṣu । tathā hi vakṣyate --
"khaṭakāvardhamānaṃ tu kṛtvā viṭagatiṃ vrajet" iti । (a 12-111) tatheti prayojana
eva prāyeṇeśvarīprasādanādau praṇāma ityarthaḥ ।
"kumudotpalakundeṣu kartavyaḥ śaṅkhadhāraṇe"
iti vā pāṭhaḥ ।</p>

<p>1anye tu1a--</p>
<lg><l>2uttāno vartulasñyaśraḥ sthito'dhomukha eva ca ।</l>
<l>3pañca pracārā hastasya nāṭyanṛttasamāśrayāḥ 4iti ।। 182</l></lg>
<lg><l>evaṃ jñeyāḥ karā hyete nānābhinayasaṃśrayāḥ5 ।</l>
<l>ata urdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi karannṛttasamāśrayān6 ।। 183</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 070 !-->
<p>hastānāṃ digbhedāvasthākṛtaṃ pracāramāha <q>uttāna</q> ityādi । uttāno yathā--'viracitamurvīsaṃstha'
mityabhinaye (9-22) patākaḥ, yathā vā jihvābhinaye āsyakṣetrago'gragāstripatākaḥ । pārśvago
yathā dhanurabhinaye muṣṭiḥ । adhomukho yathā samudrābhinaye lalāṭakṣetragaḥ । svastikapatāko, yathā
"saṃvṛtavivṛtaṃ pālya" mityatra tripatākaḥ "uttāno'dhastalasñyaśro'grago'dhomukha eva ca । pañca
pracārā hasta" syeti 1bhaṭṭodbhaṭaḥ paṭhati । tatrādhastale'dhomukho'ntarbhūtaḥ uttāne'gragaḥ, ñyaśraḥ
tripārśvaga eva । atrāpi tu samaviṣamañyaśritādyavāntarabheda uttānāderbhavati । itthaṃ traividhyameva
yuktam । tatra rasaniṣpādanamabhinayasya vastviyuktaṃ tacca karaṇānubhāvātmakaṃ, tatrāṅgahārāḥ
karaṇasañcayāḥ, karaṇasya ca lakṣaṇamuktam । "yāni sthānāni yāścāryo nṛttahastāḥ" (4-59)
ityādi । tatra sthānakacāryaḥ svakṣetre (a--13) lakṣayiṣyante ।</p>
<p>hastaprasaṅgānnṛttahastā vaktavyāḥ । kiñcābhinayakṛtāpyeṣāṃ kvacidvyākartuṃ yathā
latāhastau pratipadyete nṛttābhinayanaṃ prati (9-200), yathā vā karihastasya hastyabhinayanam ।
evaṃ catura śrādīnāmapi prayogavaśāt draṣṭavyamityāśayenāha <q>ata ūrdhva</q>miti ।

1. eṣa ślokaśca <q>kagana</q>--ādarśeṣvasti 1a--N: 'anye tu' not read in N. 2 <q>na</q>--uttāno'dhastalastryaśra
ūrdhvādhomukha eva ca <q>ḍa</q>--uttalo'dhastalastiryagūrdhvāmukha eva ca <q>ma</q>--ādarśe nāsti 3 <q>ḍa</q>--hastapracārā vijñeyā

4 <q>pa</q>--nṛttahastasamāśrayāḥ 5 <q>ma</q>--nānārtharasasambhavā <q>ḍa</q>--saṃśritāḥ <q>pa</q>--saṃjñikāḥ 6 <q>ḍa</q>--hastān nṛttasamāśrayān

<p>atha keśabandhau-keśadeśāditi । ādau pārśvakṣetrāt tatpārśvaparivartanapūrvakamutthitau*
śiraḥkṣetraṃ prāptau ata eva keśadeśānnitambahastoktavadeva vicitrahastatvena niṣkrāntau tathā tenaiva

<p>atha karihastaḥ-samunnata ityādi । saṃśleṣakrameṇa ya unnataḥ । <q>vilolita</q>

eva ca ।। 6 <q>ḍa</q>-pārśvavilokitaḥ <q>da</q>-pārśvaviloḍanaḥ 7<q>ma</q>-dvitīyaḥkaṭakākhyaśca karihastau prakīrtitau

<lg><l>1kaṭiśīrṣaniviṣṭhau dvau tripatākau yadā karau ।</l>

<lg><l>tāveva tu parāvṛttau pakṣapradyotakau3 smṛtau ।</l>
<l>4adhomukhatalāviddhau jñeyau garuḍapakṣakau ।। 201</l></lg>
<lg><l>haṃsapakṣakṛtau hastau vyāvṛttaparivartitau ।</l>

pṛthakprayoge karihastatvābhāvādityekavacanameva । tadākāratvāccedaṃ nāma* ।</p>
<p>atha pakṣavañcitau pakṣapradyotau ca-kaṭiśīrṣeti pāṭhaḥ । vṛttau pakṣāvañcitau gatau, tatsammukhau
tu taṃ dyotayatīti tathoktau । evakāreṇānayoḥ vyāmiśratayā prayogaśobhā bhavatītyāha ।</p>
<p>atha garuḍapakṣau-adhomukheti । adhomukhai nitambakṣetre bhūtvā talenāviddhau ūrdhvagamanaṃ
jhaṭiti kurvāṇau । tārkṣyabhujākārākṣepāt liṅgavākyapramāṇatvātsukaraṇaṃ prāptaṃ tripatākabādhena
patākāvupalabhyete ।</p>
<p>atha daṇḍapakṣau-haṃsapakṣakṛtāviti । ekasya haṃsapakṣasya vyāvartane vilāsena pārśvādvakṣaḥ
kṣetrasya nikaṭasya vartanaṃ tatsamakālameva dvitīyasya svedehaparivartanena vartanaṃ bhujaprasāraṇaparyantaṃ
punarapareṇāṅgeneti dvāvapi prasāritabhujau vyāvartitaparivartitau ca bhavata iti pakṣe pārśvato
daṇḍavadbhuja iti daṇḍapakṣau । yugapadeva dvayorapi prasāraṇaṃ vyāvartanaparivartane tu krameṇetyanye ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 076 !-->
1 <q>pa</q>-karihastaniviṣṭāgrau 2 <q>ma</q>-vijñeyau nāṭyakovidaiḥ 3 <q>bha</q>-pakṣoddyotakarau 4 <q>ma</q>-caturaśramuraḥ kṛtvā
1 tatsaṃmukhau kṛtam ।
*yatkīrtidharācāryeṇa tvardharecitāviti nāmasāmyena karihastāviti dvivacanāntapāṭha eva gṛhītaḥ
sādhīyāniti samarthitaśca tanmatasya khaṇḍanametadvākyam । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ-catura śrāvityādau sajātīyakaradvandvena vā,
arālakhaṭakāmukhādau vijātīyatayā vā dvivacanaṃ saṃbhāvyate । na tu karihaste yatrākṛtitvācca,
dvitīyahastaprayogagauṇatvācca, ekahastaprayoga eva dyotyate ।

<!-- COMMENTARY page 077 !-->
<p><q>athordhvamaṇḍalau -ūrdhvamaṇḍalinā</q>viti । vakṣodeśādvyāvartitakaraṇena lalāṭakṣetreṇa pārśvagamanaṃ
vidhāya tato'pi maṇḍalavadbhramaṇena prasāritāvūrdhvamaṇḍalinau । prasāritabhujāviti vartate ।
lalāṭaprāptiparyantenaivānayorlakṣaṇaṃ śiṣṭaṃ tu pārśvamaṇḍalinoriti kecit । tāveva pārśvavinyastāviti

<!-- COMMENTARY page 089 !-->
<p>bahiḥ pārṣṇikṣepācca patanamāviddhamūroḥ vartanā karaṇa iti kriyāyāṃ satyāmityanena
punaḥ punaḥ pādatalāgrāttu sthānaṃ ca kartavyamiti darśayati । ūrdhvavikṛtasya
ghaṭṭanānuddhaṭṭitaḥ udveṣṭitarūpaṃ yatkaraṇamudveṣṭyante yadāṅgulya ityādi tadeva bāhukarmabhedādbahudhā ।
tatrāsya prayoga iti vartanāśrayo viniyogaḥ। kecittu <q>prayogamāsādyā</q>nukaraṇārthamapyasya
prayoga ityūcuḥ । yathā <q>vikramorvaśyādau purūravaḥ</q> prabhṛteḥ। etena nāṭyaviṣayo viniyoga uktaḥ ।
<!-- APPARATUS page 089 !-->
1 <q>jha</q>-ityetat <q>ma</q>-etattu 2 <q>jha</q> -pādayośca 3 <q>jha</q> -udhdaṭṭitaṃ samaṃ caiva<q>da</q> N-uddhāṭitaḥ samastyśraḥ---pādaḥ
ṣoḍhā prakīrtitaḥ 3a- N -pañca prakīrtitaḥ, 4 <q>da</q> N -sthitvāgratalapādena <q>pa</q>-sthitvā pādāntalagnena

<lg><l>1somatsaritamattallī mattallī ceti ṣoḍaśa ।</l>
<l>2etā bhaubhyaḥ smṛtāścāryaḥ śrṛṇutākāśikīḥ punaḥ3 ।। 10</l></lg>
<lg><l>atikrāntā hyapakrāntā4 pārśvakrāntā5 tathaiva ca ।</l>
<l>ūrdhvajānuśca sūcī ca6 tathā nūpurapādikā ।। 11</l></lg>
<lg><l>ḍolāpādā tathākṣiptā 7āviddhodvṛttasaṃjñite ।</l>
<l>vidyudbhrāntā hyalātā ca8 bhujaṅgatrāsitā tathā ।। 12</l></lg>
<lg><l>9mṛgaplutā ca daṇḍā ca 10bhramarī10aceti ṣoḍaśa ।</l>
<l>ākāśikyaḥ smṛtā hyetā lakṣaṇaṃ ca nibodhata ।। 13</l></lg>
<lg><l>padairnirantarakṛtaistathā samanakhairapi ।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 096 !-->
śeṣaḥ । tatra nṛtte uktaṃ, yuddhe vakṣyate nyāyeṣūhyāmiti śeṣaḥ, gatau ca dvādaśādhyāye
vakṣyate--ityadhyāyatrayasyārtha iha sūcitaḥ । tatroddeśamāha--sabhāveti (bhaumyaḥ iti ?) bhūmau bhavā
bhaumyaḥ, evamākāśikyaḥ uparicaratām । smṛtā iti vedodāharaṇe'tra yāvatsmaryate tāvavdyutpādanārthaṃ
śiṣṭāni । tairvaktavyam tenaitannāśaṅkanīyam । yadi nedaṃ parigaṇanaṃ kiyatā bhedenokteti na tatra spaṣṭam ।
yallakṣaṇamanvarthaṃ ca, tavdyākriyate ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 096 !-->
1 <q>na</q>--samāsādita <q>ḍa</q>--samotsārita <q>da</q>, N --samosarita <q>ca</q> --samāsarita 2 <q>ma</q>--ādarśe ślokārdho na vartate
3 <q>na</q>--ākāśikāḥ punaḥ <q>ḍha</q>--ākāśakīḥ punaḥ 4 <q>da</q>, N --apakrāntā <q>ma</q>--tvapakrāntā 5 <q>da</q>--pārśvākrāntā
6 <q>ma</q>--ūrdhvajānustathā caiva 7 <q>ḍa</q>--vyāviddhodvṛtta <q>ma</q>--hyāviddhodvṛtta <q>ḍha</q>--hyāvṛttodvṛtta <q>ca</q>--āviddhodvṛttasaṃjñakā
8 <q>ma</q>--tathālātā <q>da</q>--hyatānā ca
9 <q>ma</q>-- utkīrṇā <q>daṇḍa</q>pādā ca bhramarī hariṇaplutā (<q>bha</q>--baddhā)
ākāśagāstvimāścāryo niyuddhakaruṇāśrayāḥ ।।
dvātriṃśadetā nirdiṣṭā mayā cāryo dvijottamāḥ ।
punarāsāṃ pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ karmaṇā saha ।।
10. <q>jha</q>--bhramarā । 10a--N: ducitaṃ ceti ṣoḍaśa

<lg><l>samapādā tu sā1 cārī vijñeyā sthānasaṃśrayā2 ।। 14</l></lg>
<lg><l>bhūmighṛṣṭena3 pādena kṛtvābhyantaramaṇḍalam ।</l>
<l>4punarutsārayedanyaṃ sthitāvartā5 tu sā smṛtā ।। 15</l></lg>
<lg><l>niṣaṇṇāṅgastu caraṇaṃ6 prasārya talasañcaram ।</l>
<l>udvāhitamuraḥ kṛtvā śakaṭāsyāṃ prayojayet ।। 16</l></lg>
<lg><l>7savyasya pṛṣṭhato vāmaścaraṇastu8 yadā bhavet ।</l>
<l>9tasyāpasarpaṇaṃ caiva jñeyā sādhyardhikā budhaiḥ10 ।। 17</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 097 !-->
<p>atha samapādā--nanu samapādā kathaṃ vā cārītyāha--<q>sthānasaṃśrayeti</q> yadā samapāda eva
stānāntaraṃ gacchati tadā caraṇaścārī bhavatyeva yogyatayā tathā vyapadeśāditi bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>atha sthitāvartā--<q>bhūmighṛṣṭeneti</q>, agratalasañcare<q>ṇābhyantaramaṇḍalaṃ</q> dvitīyapārśva jānusvastikāntaṃ,
punaḥ śabdo viśeṣaṃ dyotayan sanni(veśa)yogamāha । tena sa cet svastikatvena śliṣṭastato
dvitīyamutsārayet svāpārśvaṃ karṣayedekasya sthānamaparasyāmiti tathā ।।</p>
<p>atha śakaṭāsyā--<q>niṣaṇṇāṅgastvi</q>ti prayantaghṛtapūrvakāya ityarthaḥ । śakaṭamasanīyaṃ kṣepyaṃ
yayā । ekasminnu pāde same'ṅgulyāñcitaṃ pakṣetaraṃ kṛtvā jānanuḥ ku़ñcane jaṅghāprasaraṇe ca svapārśve ca
tyuśritatalasañcarasthāpanaṃ nu nirodhana(recana ?)miveti kecidenāmāhuḥ । etacca lakṣaṇaṃ
lakṣyārthāsaṅgatameva ।</p>
<p>athādhyārdhikā--<q>savyasyeti</q> dakṣiṇasya । <q>pṛṣṭhata</q> iti pārṣṇideśe । <q>tasye</q>ti dakṣiṇasyopasarpaṇe
svapārśvārdhatryaśritatayā sthitiḥ । avyatireketi adhyardhatālāntaratvādayo mantavyāḥ । ekasya pūrṇatā
gatiranyasya pādasya pūrṇārdhaketyanye । karaṇapradhānyāccaivamuktaṃ vāmasyāpi pṛṣṭhasaṅgatameva ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 097 !-->
1 <q>ḍa</q>--smṛtā <q>ma</q>--samapādasthitā <q>jha</q>--sṛtā 2 <q>ma</q>--saṃśritā 3 <q>ca</q>--kṛṣṭena 4 <q>ma</q>--vāmamutsārayetpādamāvartāṃ
cārimādiśet । <q>ḍa</q>--punarutsādayedanyaṃ <q>na</q>--punarutsārayetpādaṃ 5 <q>ḍa</q>--sthirāvartā <q>jha</q>--sthirāvṛttā 6 <q>ma</q>
--niṣaṇṇāgātraścaraṇaṃ <q>ḍa</q>--sadṛśaṃ 7 <q>jha</q>--savyastu 8 <q>na</q>--caraṇasya 9 <q>ma</q>--vāmāpasarpaṇāccaiva vijñeyādhyardhikā
budhaiḥ । <q>na</q>--tasyāpasarpaṇaścaiva <q>ḍa</q>--tasyopasarpaṇaṃ 10 <q>da</q>--tathā <q>ca</q>--sādhyadhikā budhaiḥ ।

<lg><l>pādaḥ prasāritaḥ savyaḥ punaścaivāpasarpitaḥ1 ।</l>
<l>vāmaḥ 2savyāpasarpī vā 3acāṣagatyāṃ3 vidhīyate ।। 18</l></lg>
<lg><l>4vicyavātsamapādāyā 5vicyavāṃ saṃprayojayet ।</l>
<l>nikuṭṭayaṃstalāgreṇa6 pādasya dharaṇītalam ।। 19</l></lg>
<lg><l>7talasañcarapādābhyāmutplutya patanaṃ tu yat ।</l>
<l>8paryāyaśaśca kriyate9 10eḍakākrīḍitā tu sā11 ।। 20</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 098 !-->
<p>atha cāṣagatiḥ--<q>savyeti</q> dakṣiṇasya pṛṣṭhata iti, savyo'pasarpatyeva sarvatra । <q>prasārita</q> iti
tālamātramagrataḥ punaḥ sa evāpasarpito dvitālamātraṃ paścānnītaḥ vāmaḥ savyena sahāpasarpati ।
kiṃcidutplutya savyavāmāvapasarpataḥ śliṣyataśceti satrāsamapasarpaṇādau cāṣasyeva gatiḥ cāṣagatiḥ ।
savyopasarpi cetyanye paṭhanti, tatra śliṣṭatvaṃ śabdo(savyo ?) ktatvamapasarpaṇaṃ cārthaḥ ।।</p>
<p>atha vicyavā--pādasyeti pādayerityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>athailakākrīḍitā--utplutyā kiṃcidekaḥ sakthigulphadeśebhyaḥ punarutplutiḥ aṅgāntareṇaivamiti
paryāyaśaḥ patanaṃ yatra cāryā sā ajikāgatitulyatvādeḍakākrīḍitā ।।</p>

1 <q>na</q>--punaścaivopasarpitaḥ 2 <q>na</q>--savyāpasarpī ca <q>da</q>--savyopasarpī vā kāśamityabhidhīyate 3 <q>ḍa</q>--cāṣagatyā
3a:N --kāśagatyā 4 <q>ma</q> --ādarśe tvadhiko'yaṃ ślokaḥ
anyonyajaṅghāsaṃvedhātsvastikā sā tu kīrtitā ।
ūrubhyāṃ valanaṃ yattu sā smṛtodvartikā budhaiḥ ।

vivṛtaṃ <q>na</q>--vicyavā <q>ḍa</q>--viśleṣaṃ <q>jha</q>--vīcivat 6 <q>ḍa</q>--tathāgreṇa 7 <q>jha</q>--talasaṃcāra <q>da</q>--nava <q>ma</q>--pādayostala--

<lg><l>1anyonyajaṅghāsaṃvedhātkṛtvā tu svastikaṃ tataḥ2 ।</l>
<l>ūrubhyāṃ valanaṃ 3yasmātsā baddhā cāryudāhṛtā4 ।। 21</l></lg>
<lg><l>talasañcarapādasya pārṣṇirbāhyonmukhī yadā5 ।</l>
<l>jaṅghāñcitā 6tathodvṛttā ūrūdvṛtteti sā smṛtā7 ।। 22</l></lg>
<lg><l>agrataḥ pṛṣṭhato vāpi 8pādo'gratalasañcaraḥ ।</l>
<l>dvitīyapādanirghṛṣṭo9 yasyāṃ syādaḍḍitā tu sā10 ।। 23</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 099 !-->
<p>atha baddhā--kevalayorevorvorvalanaṃ sthita eva jaṅghāsvastika iti baddhāṃ kecidāhuḥ । anye
tu svastikāpasaraṇena pādatalāgrayormaṇḍalabhramaṇapūrvakaṃ svasvapārśvagamanamiti yadūrubandhanamāhuḥ ।
jaḍghayoḥ saṃbandhanāt anubaddhā ।।</p>
<p>atha ūrūdvṛttā--agratalasañcarasya pādasya saṃbandhinī pārṣṇirdvitīyapādapṛṣṭhabhāgaunmukhyaṃ yadā
bhavati, jaṅghā ca jānunamanādākuñcitā udvṛttādvitīyajaṅghāsammukhaṃ valanāt tathā । ūrorūrdhvavivartanāt
lajjerṣyādiviṣayā ūrūdvṛttā । anye tu pārṣṇidvitīyasya talasañcārabāhyonmukhītyāhuḥ ।।</p>
<p>athāḍḍitā--agrata iti । apissamucyaye, vā paryāye । tena samasthitasyaikasya
dvitīyastalasañcaraḥ kramādagre pṛṣṭhe ca nirghṛṣṭaḥ śliṣṭaḥ kārya iti aḍḍitā,
<!-- APPARATUS page 099 !-->
1 <q>ma</q>--ādarśe pūrvameva niveśito'yam 2 <q>jha</q>--tu tat da--yatsyāt 3 <q>ka</q>--cāryudīritā 4 <q>ma</q>--pārṣṇiścedunmukhī
bhavet <q>da</q>--bāhyonmukhī sthitā 5 <q>ḍha</q>--tatodvṛttā 6 <q>ma</q>--sorūvṛttā tatheṣyate 7 <q>ḍa</q>--pādastu talasaṃcaraḥ 8 <q>jha</q>--pādo
nirghṛṣṭo <q>na</q>--dvitīyaṃ pādanirghṛṣṭo, 8a--N pādastu talasañcaraḥ 9 <q>ma</q>--yatra sā tvaḍḍitā bhavet । <q>jha</q>--yatra syādaḍḍitā
tathā 10 <q>bha ma</q>--ādarśayoratraiva vicyavājanitālakṣaṇamasti । 'śanai' rityādyutspanditālakṣaṇaṃ tu jānitāyā
anantarameva dṛśyate । yathā--
vicyavātsamapādāyā vicyavā sā tu kīrtitā । (<q>bha</q> --dasya)
punarnikuṭṭanaṃ caiva pādasyāgreṇa yojayet ।
pādaḥ syāttalasaṃcāraḥ karaścaiva pralambitaḥ ।
muṣṭihastaśca vakṣaḥstho janitā sā vidhīyate ।।
śanaiḥ pādavivarto yo bāhyenābhyantareṇa vā ।
recatasyānucaraṇājjñeyā cāskanditā budhaiḥ ।।

<lg><l>1śanaiḥ pādo nivarteta2 bāhyenābhyantareṇa ca ।</l>
<l>yadrecakānusāreṇa3 sā cāryutspanditā4 smṛtā ।। 24</l></lg>
<lg><l>5muṣṭihastaśca vakṣassthaḥ karo'nyaśca pravartitaḥ6 ।</l>
<l>7talasañcarapādaśca janitā cāryudāhṛtā ।। 25</l></lg>
<lg><l>8pañcatālāntaraṃ pādaṃ prasārya syanditāṃ9 nyaset ।</l>
<l>dvitīyena tu pādena10 tathāpasyanditāmapi ।। 26</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 100 !-->
pādasya svasthānātikramaṇāt । aḍḍa atikramahiṃsayoriti paṭhanti,sattve ca rūpam*।। madhusūdanī
reads: aḍḍa atikramahiṃsayorityasya itaci rūpaṃ paṭhanti sattve ca and observes isī
aḍḍa dhātu kā bhāva meṃ yaha rūpa hai । yahām̐ 'sattve' kā artha bhāva hai ।</p>
<p>athotspanditā--bāhyena kaniṣṭhāṅgulibhāgena abhyantarāṅguṣṭhabhāgena nivartate cedu(bhayoḥ pādayoḥ)
gamāgamaṃ kurute । kimavadhītyāha pādarecitasyāpasāreṇa śobhāpekṣayotkrāntamasyām । yannadyāḥ
pratyāvartanarūpaspanditakṛt tattulyatvādiyamutspanditā । recakaṃ nṛttahastamatra kecidāhuḥ ।।</p>
<p>atha janitā--<q>talasañcarapādaḥ pravartita</q> iti । etadevāsyāḥ svarūpaṃ muṣṭervakṣogāmitvaṃ
hastāntarasya ca pravartanamitikartavyatāmātram । samastagatīnāmiyaṃ jananaṃ karoti prārambharūpatvāditi
janitā ।+</p>
<p>atha syanditāpasyandite --kramasamo niṣaṇṇoruḥ pādo dakṣiṇastu pañcatālān prasāritaḥ ।
"tālaḥ smṛtaḥ madhyamayā" iti । sā syanditā prasāraṇadharmatvāt । etadviparyayādasyā api savyena
syanditeneti aṅgaparyāyācca labdhāpyeṣā prayoge sāhacaryaniyamakhyāpanārthaṃ punarnirūpitā ।
ālīḍhapratyālīḍhayostu pādadvayamapi tryaśritasaṃsthānaṃ maṇḍalasthānato jīvitvaṃ yadvakṣyate 'asyaiva

1 <q>na</q>--vivarteta 2 <q>da</q>--kāreṇa 3 <q>da</q> --sā cāsracchanditā 4 <q>ca</q>--cāryutsanditā 5 <q>da</q>--svastihastastu
6 <q>ca</q>--karo'nyaśca prakīrtitaḥ <q>na</q>--karo'nyaścāpavartitaḥ <q>pa</q>--karo'nyaḥ parivartitaḥ । 7 <q>da</q>--talāgrasaṃsthitaḥ pādoḥ
janitāyāmudāhṛtā

dvitīyaṃ ca nayetpārśvaṃ sāvaskandeti cocyate ।।

<lg><l>1talasañcarapādābhyāṃ 2ghūrṇamānopasarpaṇaiḥ ।</l>
<l>3samotsaritamattallī vyāyāme samudāhṛtā ।। 27</l></lg>
<lg><l>ubhābhyāmapi pādābhyāṃ ghūrṇamānopasarpaṇaiḥ ।</l>
<l>udveṣṭitāpaviddhaiśca 4hastairmattallyudāhṛtā ।। 28</l></lg>
<lg><l>etā 5bhaumyaḥ smṛtāścāryo 6niyuddhakaruṇāśrayāḥ ।</l>
<l>7ākāśikīnāṃ cārīṇāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। 29</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 101 !-->
dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ pañcatālān' ityādi syanditāyāstu naivamiti śeṣaḥ । sthānasya sthitipradhānatā
cāryāstu gatipradhānatetyapi viśeṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>atha samotsaritamattallī--talasañcarajaṅghāsvastikenābhyantare yadānyasya tadeva ca
dvitīyatalasañcaraṃ karoti tato ghūrṇamānayostayoḥ upasarpaṇamityanye । samaḥ avikalaḥ । (a)
avanaṃ rakṣaṇaṃ ut tadarthaṃ saritaḥ gatimān madanaṃ mat madaṃ tanotīti mattat tasya layo gamanaṃ
yasyāmiti samotsaritamattallī । saritaśabdo ri gatau vinyasyate sahena samāse ca madanaṃ mutkṣipaḥ
layanaṃ līḥ । sariśabdasya pratipadikāt tṛci vā saritaśabdaḥ । saṃ ā ut sarita ityanye
paṭhanti*। madena yo na vikalībhūtaḥ rakṣārthaṃ cānyataraḥ palāyate tasya vai dvidhā gatiriti
madhyamadaviṣayeyaṃ cārī sampadyate ।</p>
<p>atha mattallī--<q>pādābhyā</q>miti bhūmiśliṣṭāśeṣatālākhyāmiti jaṅghāsvastika--
yogenārdhatryaśribhāgābhyāṃ ghūrṇamānatvenāpasarpaṇādvā, agāḍha(? gāḍha) madaviṣayā mattallī ।</p>
<p><q>niyuddhakaraṇāśrayā</q> iti niyuddhe'nādisiddhā etāḥ karaṇāṅgahāreṣu ca tato nāṭye ।
smṛtā ityānenopavedasaṃbandhatvena vedo'tra pramāṇamiti darśitaṃ, viniyogadikpradarśanaṃ cedaṃ mantavyam ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 101 !-->
1 <q>bhama</q>--ādarśayoḥ pratijñāpāṭhānusāreṇa mattallyā anantarameva samosaritamattallīlakṣaṇaṃ vartate । <q>yathā</q>--
añcitena tu pādena ghūrṇamānopasarpaṇaiḥ । udveṣṭitāpaviddhatvānmattallī karayormatā ।। ubhayoḥ pādayoścāpi
ghūrṇamānāpasarpaṇaiḥ । samotsāritamattallī vyāyāme sā vidhīyate ।। 2 <q>ḍa</q>--ghūrṇamānāpasarpaṇaiḥ 3 <q>pa</q>--samosarita
4 <q>cha</q>--karaiḥ 5 <q>ḍa</q>--bhūmyaḥ <q>ma</q>--bhūmigatāḥ 6 <q>ḍa</q>--niyukta 7 <q>ma</q>--śastramokṣāṅgāreṣu vakṣyāmyākāśagāḥ punaḥ ।
<q>na</q>--ākāśikānāṃ
*'osaria' ityapasaraṇārthakaprākṛtarūpasya saṃskṛtīkaraṇamiti kecit । tatrāpaśabdadoṣaṃ parijihīrṣuṇācāryeṇa
bhaṅgībhedena niruktiranugṛhīteti manyāmahe ।

<lg><l>1akuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya purataḥ saṃprasārayet1 ।</l>
<l>utkṣipya pātayeccainamatikrāntā tu2 sā smṛtā ।। 30</l></lg>
<lg><l>3ūrubhyāṃ valanaṃ kṛtvā kuñcitaṃ 4pādamuddharet ।</l>
<l>pārśve vinikṣipeccainamapakrāntā tu sā smṛtā5 ।। 31</l></lg>
<lg><l>kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya 9jānustanasamaṃ nyaset6 ।</l>
<l>uddhaṭṭitena pādena pārśvakrāntā vidhīyate8 ।। 32</l></lg>
<lg><l>kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya 9jānustanasamaṃ nyaset10 ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 102 !-->
<p>athātikrāntā--<q>utkṣiptā yasya pārṣṇi</q>riti (9--277) kuñcitaṃ taddvitīyagulphakṣetre
kṛtvā kiṃcit purataḥ prasārya prakṛtibhedena catustālādyantaramutkṣipyāgreṇa bhūmau nipātyata iti
gantavyātikramādatikrāntā ।1</p>
<p>athāpakrāntā--ūrū ca stanopalakṣitāṃ pūrvaṃ (baddhāṃ) kṛtvā tataḥ pādamudghṛtya pārśve
kṣipedityapakramaṇādapakrāntā2 ।</p>
<p>atha pārśva<q>krāntā</q>--kuñcitaṃ pādaṃ svapārśvenopari nītvā bhūmau pāṣṇaryā pātayediti pūrvaṃ
ku़ñcanādbalādevodghāṭitatvaṃ bhavati, tasya hi lakṣaṇaṃ "sthitvā pādatalāgreṇa pārṣṇīrbhūmau nipātyata"
iti (9--266)iyameva pārṣṇicaṇḍaghāteti prasiddhā । anye tu dvitīyarukṣetraṃ yāvadutkṣipyodghāṭitena
pātayedityāhuḥ ।।</p>
<p>athordhvajānuḥ--<q>kramastabdha</q>miti yathā tasyotkṣepastathāsya stabdhatetyarthaḥ ।</p>

1 <q>ma</q>--saṃprayojayet <q>na</q>--saṃprakārayet 1a--N: pādasya nirgamaṃ kṛtvā tathopāṅgāni yojayet 2 <q>ma</q>--pātayeccaikamati
krānteti । 3 <q>bha</q>--ūrdhvāvalitakaṃ <q>da</q>--N ūrvorvalitakaṃ <q>ma</q>--ūrubhyāṃ valitaṃ 4 <q>ḍa</q>--tu samuddharet 5
<q>ma</q>--prakīrtitā 6 <q>na</q>--jānūrdhvaṃ saṃprasārayet <q>ḍa</q>--pārśvotthānodgatirbhavet <q>da</q> N --pārśvotthānotthitaṃ nyaset

<lg><l>1kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya ñyaśramūruṃ vivartayet2 ।</l>

<p>atha daṇḍapādā--nūpurapādoktaṃ kuñcitaṃ pādaṃ dvitīyapārṣṇigaṃ kṛtvāgrataḥ prasārayet; <q>kathaṃ,

<lg><l>1atikrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā trikaṃ tu parivartayet ।</l>

<p>itikartavyatāśeṣaṃ viniyogādikaṃ cāsāṃ darśayati--<q>lalitāṅgakriyātmikā</q> iti dhanurvajretyādi

(10--73) iti tatprādhānyaṃ yadā bhavati tadā prayojanā kīdṛśī kāryeti spaṣṭayitumāha--<q>yato

sthānakāni ṣaṭ ।

<lg><l>1dvau tālāvardhatālaśca pādayorantaraṃ bhavet ।</l>
<l>tayossamutthitastvekasatryaśraḥ pakṣasthito'paraḥ ।। 52</l></lg>
<lg><l>kiṃcidañcitajaṅghaṃ ca2 sauṣṭhavāṅgapuraskṛtam3 ।</l>

añcitā kuṭilā jānunāmanājjaṅghā yatra । sauṣṭhave yadaṅgaṃ vakṣyate tena puraskṛtaṃ pūjitaṃ, sauṣṭhava
apradhāne vā aṅgapuraskṛtaṃ pradhānam । <q>hi</q> yasmāt <q>viṣṇuratrādhidaivatam</q> tasmādvaiṣṇavam । tena tasya

1 <q>bhama</q>yorvaiṣṇavalakṣaṇaṃ tu
svabhāvasaṃsthistvekastryaśraḥ pakṣasthito'paraḥ ।
kiṃcittathāñcitā jaṅghā samunnatamurastathā ।।
hanuśīrṣe same caiva karṇādaṣṭāṅgale sthite ।
uraḥ sthānācca cibukaṃ caturaṅgalasaṃsthitam ।।
kaṭakastripatāko vā dakṣiṇo nābhisaṃsthitaḥ।
tripatāko'rdhacandro vā vāmaḥ kaṭitaṭāśritaḥ ।।
pādayorantaraṃ yattattaladvayamitaṃ bhavet ।
jñeyaṃ tadvaiṣṇavaṃ sthānaṃ <q>kāryamuttamamadhyayoḥ</q> ।। (viṣṇuratrādhidaivatam--<q>ma</q>)
sthānenānena kartavyaḥ sallāpastu svabhāvajaḥ ।
śeṣaṃ kāryamanenaiva yadavasthena karmaṇā ।।
2 <q>ḍa</q>--jaṅgho'sau <q>ḍha</q>--jaṅghaśca 3 <q>na</q>--samanvitam <q>ḍhaḍa</q>--samanvitaḥ 4 <q>na</q>--prabhāvataḥ 5 <q>na</q>--nānākāryāntaropeto
6 <q>nada</q>--ādarśayoḥ "cakrasya" ādi "yojitam" iti paryanto bhāgo na vartate । 7 <q>ca</q>--dhanuṣi sthite 8 <q>jajha</q>yostrayaḥ
ślokā na santi <q>ḍa</q>--dhairyadānāṅga <q>ḍha</q>--dhairyādānāṅga 9 <q>ca</q>--tathodvāhyaḥ ।

darśitā । mābhūdevaṃ kālapramāṇa(kalāparimāṇa?) niyamābhidhānaṃ gajasnānībhūtamityāha <q>uttamānāṃ

<lg><l>uttamānāmiyaṃ kāryā puruṣāṇāṃ gatirbudhaiḥ ।</l>
<l>madhyamānāṃ gatiṃ caiva saṃpravakṣyāmyahaṃ punaḥ ।। 69</l></lg>
<lg><l>jvarāteṃ ca rujārte ca tapaḥśrānte bhayānvite ।</l>
<l>vikṣate cchannagamane tvavahitthe tathaiva ca ।। 70</l></lg>
<lg><l>cintānvite tathā svastha autsukye saṃhate tathā ।</l>
<l>gatiḥ sthiralayā kāryāṃ karaṇāśrayabhāvinī ।। 71</l></lg>
<lg><l>bhaye vitrāsite caiva pramatte śaṅkite tathā ।</l>
<l>vyādhite harṣite krodhe kāryaṃ tu caturāñcitam ।। 72</l></lg>
<lg><l>saṃbhramādbhutasaṃdarśe muhurmuhuravekṣaṇaiḥ ।</l>
<l>kampanena ca gātrāṇāṃ vastrasyākarṣaṇena ca ।। 73</l></lg>
<lg><l>susandhitā cūrṇapadā śakārasya gatirbhavet ।</l>
<l>sthūlasyāpi tu kartavyā gatirdehānukarṣiṇī ।। 74</l></lg>
<lg><l>samuddhāhitagātrā ca vilambitapadakramā ।</l>
<l>viṣkambhagāminī caiva niśvāsabahulā tathā ।। 75</l></lg>
<lg><l>atikrāntā ca kartavyā tathā cūrṇapadaiḥ sadā ।</l>
<l>kāryā caiva tu hīnānāṃ ceṭyādīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 76</l></lg>

<pb n="182"/>

<lg><l>adhamā iti ye khyātā nānāśīlāḥ kuvṛttayaḥ ।</l>
<l>pārśvamekaṃ śiraścaiva karaṃ caraṇameva ca ।। 77</l></lg>
<lg><l>nāmayettadgatau kiṃcitkujanmā ceṭasaṃjñitaḥ ।</l>
<l>jātinīceṣu kartavyā vilokanaparā gatiḥ ।। 78</l></lg>
<lg><l>vikalā bakasaṃcārā gātraṃ sarvaṃ niyamya ca ।</l>
<l>svajātisadṛśī caiva tathā dehānukarṣiṇī ।। 79</l></lg>
<lg><l>saṃbhrame caiva harṣe ca vikṣiptapadavikramā ।</l>
<l>āsādya hāsyaṃ tu rasametāścānyāśca yojayet ।। 80</l></lg>
<lg><l>punaśca karuṇe kāryā gatiḥ sthirapadakramā ।</l>
<l>sabāṣpaḥ sāśrunayanaḥ sannagātrastathaiva ca ।। 81</l></lg>
<lg><l>utkṣiptapātitakaraḥ tathā sasvanarodanaiḥ ।</l>
<l>gacchedathādhyardhikayā pratyagrāpriyasaṃśrayāt ।। 82</l></lg>
<lg><l>eṣā strīṣu prayoktavyā nīcasattveṣu caiva hi ।</l>
<l>uttamānāṃ tu kartavyā sabāṣpā dhairyasaṃyutā ।। 83</l></lg>
<lg><l>niśvāsairāyatotsṛṣṭaistathā cordhvanirīkṣaṇaiḥ ।</l>
<l>na tatra sauṣṭhavaṃ kāryaṃ na pramāṇaṃ yathoditam । 84</l></lg>
<lg><l>nātyutkṣiptaiḥ padairgacchediṣṭabandhunipātane ।</l>
<l>gāḍhaprahāre kāryā ca śithilāṅgabhujāśrayā ।। 85</l></lg>
<lg><l>vighūrṇitaśarīrā ca gatiścūrṇapadairatha ।</l>
<l>gatiḥ kāñcukinī proktā vayo'vasthā viśeṣataḥ ।। 86</l></lg>
<lg><l>vṛddhe vā madhyame vāpi tathā caiva kanīyasi ।</l>
<l>ardhatālotthitaiḥ pādairviṣkambhairṛjubhistadā ।। 87</l></lg>
<lg><l>udvahanniva gātrāṇi paṅkamagna iva vrajet ।</l>
<l>atha vṛddhasya kartavyā gatiḥ kampitadehikā ।। 88</l></lg>
<lg><l>viṣkambhitagatiprāṇā mandotkṣiptapadā tathā ।</l>
<l>śītena cābhibhūtasya varṣeṇābhihatasya ca ।। 89</l></lg>
<lg><l>gati prayoktṛbhiḥ kuryātstrīnīcaprakṛtaiḥ sadā ।</l>
<l>piṇḍīkṛtya ca gātrāṇi teṣāṃ caiva prakampanāt ।। 90</l></lg>

<pb n="183"/>

<lg><l>karau vakṣasi nikṣipya kubjadehā tathaiva ca ।</l>
<l>dantoṣṭhasphuraṇāccaiva cibukasya prakampanāt ।। 91</l></lg>
<lg><l>śanaiḥ śanaiśca kartavyā śītārtābhinaye gatiḥ ।</l>
<l>uṣṇe cāpi prayoktāvyā gatirdāhasamākulā ।। 92</l></lg>
<lg><l>netrasaṃkocanasvedagātrasaṃharaṇānvitā ।</l>
<l>atikrāntairapakrāntairelakākrīḍitaistathā ।। 93</l></lg>
<lg><l>kramairabhinayairyuktā tathā cūrṇapadairapi ।</l>
<l>etānanyāṃśca yuñjīta nāṭyajñaiḥ karuṇe rase ।। 94</l></lg>
<lg><l>raudre rase pravakṣyāmi daityarakṣogaṇānprati ।</l>
<l>eka eva rasasteṣāṃ sthāyī raudro dvijottamāḥ ।। 95</l></lg>
<lg><l>nepathyaraudro vijñeyaḥ svāṅgaraudrastathaiva ca ।</l>
<l>atha svabhāvajaścaiva tridhā raudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 96</l></lg>
<lg><l>rudhiraklinnadeho yo raudrābhivikṛtānanaiḥ ।</l>
<l>tathā piśitahastaśca raudro naipathyajastu saḥ ।। 97</l></lg>
<lg><l>bahubāhurbamukho nānāpraharaṇākulaḥ ।</l>
<l>sthūlakāyastvatiprāṃśuraṅgaraudrastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। 98</l></lg>
<lg><l>raktākṣaḥ piṅgakeśaśca kṛṣṇāṅgo vikṛtasvaraḥ ।</l>
<l>raudranirbhartsanakatho raudro'yaṃ syātsvabhāvajaḥ ।। 99</l></lg>
<lg><l>catustālottarotkṣiptaiḥ pādaistryantarapatitaiḥ ।</l>
<l>gatirevaṃ prakartavyā śeṣā ye cāpi tadvidhāḥ ।। 100</l></lg>
<lg><l>eka eva rasasteṣāṃ sthāyī raudro dvijottamāḥ ।</l>
<l>vigrahaḥ prahasaścaiva tathā śrṛṅgāra iṣyate ।। 101</l></lg>
<lg><l>tathā bhayānake cāpi gatiḥ kāryā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।</l>
<l>strīṇāṃ kāpuruṣāṇāṃ ca ye cānye sattvavarjitāḥ ।। 102</l></lg>
<lg><l>viṣphā (?sphā)ritacalannetro vidhunvan svaśirastathā ।</l>
<l>bhayākulitacittatvātpārśvāni ca vilokayan ।। 103</l></lg>
<lg><l>drutaiścūrṇapadaiścaiva kṛtvā hastaṃ kapotakam ।</l>
<l>prale (?ve) pitaśarīrastu śuṣkoṣṭhaśca skhalanvrajet ।। 104</l></lg>

<pb n="184"/>

<lg><l>eṣānukaraṇe kāryā tarjane kalahe tathā ।</l>
<l>sattvaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca vikṛtasvaram ।। 105</l></lg>
<lg><l>eṣā strīṇāṃ prayoktavyā nṝṇāṃ cākṣiptavikramā ।</l>
<l>kvacidāsannapatitairvikṛṣṭapatitaiḥ kvacit ।। 106</l></lg>
<lg><l>eḻa(? la)kākrīḍitaiḥ pādairuparyuparipātitaiḥ ।</l>
<l>eṣāmevānugairhastairgatirbhīteṣu yojayet ।। 107</l></lg>
<lg><l>ahṛdyā tu mahī yatra śmaśānaraṇakaśmalā ।</l>
<l>gatistatra prakurvīta bībhatsābhinayaṃ prati ।। 108</l></lg>
<lg><l>kvacidāsannapatitairvikṛṣṭapatitaiḥ kvacit ।</l>
<l>atikrāntaiḥ padairgacchejjugupsitagatiṃ prati ।। 109</l></lg>
<lg><l>tathā vīre ca kartavyā pādavikṣepasaṃyutā ।</l>
<l>drutapracāraṇāviddhā nānācārīsamākulā ।। 110</l></lg>
<lg><l>pārśvākrāntairdrutāviddhaiḥ sūcīviddhaistathaiva ca ।</l>
<l>kalātāḻa(?la) gataiḥ pādairāvege yojayedgatim ।। 111</l></lg>
<lg><l>viṭasyāpi tu kartavyā gatirlalitavikramā ।</l>
<l>kiṃcidākuñcitaiḥ pādaistāḻā(? lā)bhyantarapātitaiḥ ।। 112</l></lg>
<lg><l>raṅgasauṣṭhavasaṃyuktaṃ tathā hastau kaṭisthitau ।</l>
<l>khaṭakāvardhamānau ca kṛtvā kāryā viṭe gatiḥ ।। 113</l></lg>
<lg><l>kṛśāṅgānāṃ tu kartavyā gatirmandaparikramā ।</l>
<l>vyādhigrasto jvarārtaśca tapaśśrāntaḥ kṣudhānvitaḥ ।। 114</l></lg>
<lg><l>viṣṭambhanagataprāṇastathā kṣāmodaraḥ sadā ।</l>
<l>kṣāmasvarakapolaśca sannagātrastathaiva ca ।। 115</l></lg>
<lg><l>hastapādasamutkṣepaṃ śanaistatra prayojayet ।</l>
<l>kampanaṃ caiva gātrāṇāṃ ślathanaṃ caiva yojayet ।। 116</l></lg>
<lg><l>prakartavyādhvagasyāpi gatirmandaparikramā ।</l>
<l>vikūṇanena vaktrasya jānunośca vimarśanān ।। 117</l></lg>
<lg><l>nīcānāṃ madhyamānāṃ ca gatiḥ kāryā sadā budhaiḥ ।</l>
<l>tālamātrotthitaiḥ pādaistathā vyākuñcitāñcitaiḥ ।। 118</l></lg>

<pb n="185"/>

<lg><l>yatinaścāśramasthā ye ye cānye tapasi sthitāḥ ।</l>
<l>ṛṣayastāpasāścaiva naiṣṭhikaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ ।। 119</l></lg>
<lg><l>ālolacakṣuḥ syāccaiva yugamātranirīkṣaṇe ।</l>
<l>upasthitasmṛtiścaiva gātraṃ sarvaṃ niyamya ca ।। 120</l></lg>
<lg><l>acañcalamanāścaiva gacchelliṅgasamāśritaḥ ।</l>
<l>vinītaveṣaśca tathā kāṣāyavasano'pi ca ।। 121</l></lg>
<lg><l>prathamaṃ samapādena sthitvā sthānena nāṭyavit ।</l>
<l>hastaṃ caturakaṃ kṛtvā tathā caitatprasārayet ।। 122</l></lg>
<lg><l>prasannavadanaṃ kṛtvā prayogasya vaśānugam ।</l>
<l>suniṣaṇṇena gātreṇa gatiṃ kuryādyatestathā ।। 123</l></lg>
<lg><l>uttamānāṃ bhavedeṣā liṅgināṃ ye mahāvratāḥ ।</l>
<l>ebhireva viparyastairguṇairanyeṣu liṅgiṣu ।। 124</l></lg>
<lg><l>tathā vratānugā ca syādanyeṣāṃ liṅgināṃ gatiḥ ।</l>
<l>hastau tadanugau cāpi yathāyogaṃ prayojayet ।। 125</l></lg>
<lg><l>1vibhrāntā vā hyudāttā ca vikrāntā vihṛtā tathā ।</l>
<l>śakaṭāsyasthitaiḥ pādairatikrāntaistathaiva ca ।। 126</l></lg>
<lg><l>kāryā pāśupatānāṃ ca gatirudbhrāntagāminī ।</l>
<l>2evaṃ liṅgasthitānāṃ hi prayojyaiva gatirbudhaiḥ ।। 127</l></lg>
<lg><l>andhasyeva gatiṃ kuryādandhakāreṣu yogavat ।</l>
<l>bhūmau visarpitaiḥ pādairhastadarśitamārgakaiḥ ।। 128</l></lg>
<lg><l>rathasthasyāpi kartavyā gatiścūrṇapadakramā ।</l>
<l>samapādaṃ tathā sthānaṃ kṛtvā rathagatiṃ vrajet ।। 129</l></lg>
<lg><l>dhanurekena hastena gṛhītvānyena sāyakam ।</l>
<l>sūtaścāsya bhavedevaṃ pratodapragrahākulaḥ ।। 130</l></lg>
<lg><l>karaṇāni vacitrāṇi kartavyāni vibhāgataḥ ।</l>

<pb n="186"/>

<lg><l>vimānasthasya kartavyā gatī rathagatopamā ।</l>

<lg><l>asyaiva vaiparītyena kuryāccāpyavarohaṇam ।</l>
<l>adho'valokanenaiva maṇḍalāvartanena ca ।। 133</l></lg>
<lg><l>ākāśagamane caiva kartavyaṃ gaticaiṣṭitam ।</l>
<l>sthānena samapādena tathā cūrṇapadairatha ।। 134</l></lg>
<lg><l>vyomnastvavataredyastu tasyemāṃ kāreyadgatim ।</l>
<l>ṛjvāyatonnatanataiḥ kuṭilāvartitaistathā ।। 135</l></lg>
<lg><l>bhramamāṇasya cākāśādaparuddhabhujāgatiḥ ।</l>
<l>vikīrṇavasanā caiva tathā bhūgatalocanā । 136</l></lg>
<lg><l>drumaprāsādaśaileṣu nadīnimnonnateṣu ca ।</l>
<l>ārohaṇāvataraṇaṃ kāryamarthavaśādbudhaiḥ ।। 137</l></lg>
<lg><l>prāsādārohaṇaṃ kāryamatikrāntaiḥ padairatha ।</l>

<lg><l>tathāvataraṇe caiva gātramānamya recayet ।</l>

<lg><l>prāsādārohaṇaṃ yattu taddevādiṣu kārayet ।</l>

<lg><l>drume cārohaṇaṃ kāryamatikrāntotthitaiḥ padaiḥ ।</l>
<l>sūcīviddhairapakrāntaiḥ pārśvakrāntaistathaiva ca ।। 141</l></lg>
<lg><l>evaṃ devāvataraṇaṃ prayojyaṃ saridādiṣu ।</l>
<l>prāsādeṣu tathā proktaṃ tathaivottaraṇaṃ bhavet ।। 142</l></lg>
<lg><l>drumaprāsādaśailāṃśca saṃjñāmātreṇa darśayet ।</l>
<l>1jalapramāṇāpekṣā tu jalamadhye gatirbhavet ।। 143</l></lg>
<lg><l>toye'lpe vasanotkarṣaiḥ prājye pāṇivikarṣaṇaiḥ ।</l>

<pb n="187"/>

<lg><l>prasārya bāhumekaikaṃ muhurvārivikarṣaṇaiḥ ।</l>

<lg><l>aśvayāne gatiḥ kāryā vaiśākhasthānakena tu ।</l>

<lg><l>pannagānāṃ gatiḥ kāryā pādaiḥ svastikasaṃsthitaiḥ ।</l>

<lg><l>2ākāśaskhalitaiḥ prāyaḥ pādaiścāpyanavasthitaiḥ ।</l>

<lg><l>unmattasyāpi kartavyā gatistvaniyamakramā ।</l>

<lg><l>pragītahasitaścāpi nānāvikṛtabhūṣaṇaḥ ।</l>

<pb n="188"/>

<lg><l>sthitvā nūpurapādena daṇḍapādaṃ prasārayet ।</l>
<l>kṛtvā cārīṃ tathodbaddhāmatha svastikameva ca ।। 158</l></lg>
<lg><l>anena cārīyogena paribhrāmya tu maṇḍalam ।</l>

<lg><l>trikaṃ salalitaṃ kṛtvā latākhyaṃ hastameva ca ।</l>

<lg><l>siṃharkṣavānarāṇāṃ ca gatiḥ kāryā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।</l>
<l>1yā kṛtā narasiṃhena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ।। 161</l></lg>
<lg><l>ālīḍhasthānakaṃ kṛtvā gātraṃ tasyaiva cānugam ।</l>
<l>ūrdhvajānu ca vikṣipya karamekaṃ ca saṃsthitam ।। 162</l></lg>
<lg><l>vilolitaṃ śiraḥ kṛtvā cibukaṃ bāhumastake ।</l>
<l>gantavyaṃ vikramaiścaiva pañcatālāntarasthitaiḥ ।। 163</l></lg>
<lg><l>2niyuddhe saṃśaye caiva raṅgāvataraṇe tathā ।</l>
<l>siṃhādīnāṃ ca yoktavyā gatireṣā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। 164</l></lg>
<lg><l>śeṣāṇāmarthayogena sthānānyapi tu kārayet ।</l>
<l>gajavājirathādīṃstu cihnamātreṇa kārayet ।। 165</l></lg>

<p>iti śrībhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre gatipracāro nāma
dvādaśo'dhyāyaḥ ।</p>

vṛttisaṃśritaiśca 1prayogairabhihitā deśāḥ, 2yataḥ pravṛtticatuṣṭayamabhinirvṛttaṃ

pratyekaṃ tatraivābhyupagamaḥ pravṛttiḥ, netyāha lokānuguṇānusāreṇa । loko hi dakṣiṇāpathaḥ pūrvadeśaḥ
paścimadeśaḥ uttarabhūmiriti 1caturdhā vibhāgo'sti, na caiṣa nirbandhanaḥ sādṛśyasaṃbhavāt । tathāhi
dākṣiṇātyeṣu śrṛṅgārapracuratayā kaiśikyāḥ saṃbhavaḥ । paścimeṣvāvantyeva saṃgṛhīteṣu sāpi sati
dharmaprādhānya iti sāttvatyasti । prācyeṣu tu ghaṭāṭopavākyāḍambaraprādhānyo bhāratyārabhaṭīyogaḥ ।
uttarabhūmiḥ prādhānyāttu bhāratyārabhaṭīyoge'pi kaiśikīleśāttu praveśasahiṣṇavo yadvakṣyate
''prayogastvalpagītārtha'' (13--51) iti । arthaśabdena tatprayojanaṃ nṛttavādyādi । ityevaṃ

<p>evamantaraṅgopakāritvātkakṣyāmādhāramuktvā tadākṣiptaṃ ca vṛttibhedamabhidhāya dharmā (rmyo)
(madhusūdanī, pṛ. 1338) nirūpyante । tathā hi lokasvabhāvamevānuvartamānaṃ dharmidvayam । loko
nāma janapadavāsī janaḥ, sa ca pravṛttikrameṇa prapañcitaḥ । tatprasaṅgenaiva tāvaddharmyāyātā । sā
cāṅgikaśeṣatayā vaktavyā । prasaṅgācca vācikāhāryādiviṣayāṇyucyante tulyalakṣaṇatvāditi । sā
ca dvedhā । yadyapi laukikadharmavyatirekeṇa nāṭye na kaściddharmo'sti, tathāpi sa yatra
lokāgataprakriyākramo rañjanādhikyaprādhānyamadhirohayituṃ kavinaṭavyāpāre vaicitryaṃ svīkurvan
nāṭyadharmītyucyate ।</p>

5 <q>ma</q>--yojyānyetāni mānuṣaiḥ 6 "yato mukhamitiślokaḥ tadanantaraṃ" 'athādi'....kāryaḥ, iti antaṃ ṣaṭślokāḥ <q>kā</q>di

<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati--yadā kaviryathāvṛttavastumātraṃ varṇayati naṭaśca prayuṅkte, na tu svabuddhikṛtaṃ

<p>atha nāṭyadharmī lakṣayati <q>ativākyakriyopeta</q>miti । itihāsādivākyamatikramya yā

yathā tāpasavatsarājena mantrisamucitagāmbhīryāvahitthayojanaṃ vasantakasya tathā, svabhāvabhāṣita--
matikramya yatsthitaṃ yathā rājñyāḥ saṃskṛtam* । evaṃbhūtaṃ kāvyaṃ kāvyagatanāṭyadharmī naṭagatā tu
nāṭyalakṣaṇalakṣitaṃ kṛtvā līlayā śobhāpradhānatayā aṅgahārāṇi manoharāṇi
tatpradhānairabhinayaiḥ upetaṃ tathāpāṭhe svarālaṅkārasaṃyojanā yuktaṃ yatra ca puruṣo na

<p>caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ*</p>
<lg><l>yo vāgabhinayaḥ 1pūrvaṃ mayā prokto dvijottamāḥ ।</l>

<p>atha caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>dvidhāsthitaṃ sadma sadāvibhaktaṃ viśvānpadārthān1 samupādadānam ।</l>
<l>pāṇīndriyaṃ 2saṃvyavahārahetu ( ?hetuṃ) yasyeśvaraṃ taṃ varadaṃ namāmaḥ ।।</l></lg>
<p>āṅgikābhinayānantaraṃ vācikasya bheda3 nāṭyānuprāṇakatayā pūrvoddiṣṭāṅgikasya
viṣayasamarpaṇaprāṇatvācca vāciko lakṣaṇīya ityevaṃbhūtāmadhyāyasaṅgatiṃ karoti <q>yo vāgabhinaya</q>
iti । vāgevābhinayaḥ vācikābhinayaḥ । <q>pūrva</q>miti ṣaṣṭhe'dhyāye 4sa nirūpyate, 5tattvena
cāsyābhidhānaprādhānyāt । atra hetumāha <q>vāci yatnastu kartavya</q> iti kavinā nirmāṇakāle naṭena
prayogakāle । kuta ityāha (<q>nāṭyasyaiṣeti</q>) eṣā hi tanurnāṭyasya sakalaprayogabhittibhūtatvenātodya--

<p>*nāma yathā madanaripuriti bhagavatparyāyaśceti tadīyaśṛṅgāravarṇane na prayojyam । ākhyātamapi
yadvaicitryamāvahati, "smara si smara mekhalāguṇaiḥ"* iti vartamānapratyayena
1tatsākṣātkaraṇamupālambhaviṣayatā, tvamevātra sākṣī anṛtaṃ na prakaṭitaṃ, anyathā smṛtavāniti
mekhalāguṇairiti syāt । upasargātprakṛtārthayogino yathā--nirmita ityarthe na mitiḥ । adhikadyotako
yathā-- "muhurupacitairdṛṣṭirālupyate" †iti । upasargaiḥ karmapravacanīyā apyupalakṣyante (yathā) "kiṃ
syādarjunataḥ prati" iti, "vicitaṃ nāstīti" pratītiḥ punareva syāt, arjunakṛte vicitamiti ।
taddhitapratyayopalakṣaṇam ।

na tu cittaṃ vicārayatyātmana eveti । evaṃ subdhātupratyayapadaṃ na talsu kṛtsu vācyaṃ gauravabhayāttu
nodāhṛtam ।</p>
<p>strīpratyayo yathā-- 'adhyāsīnaḥ savaidagdhī' 2karma tayā kṛtī na tu vaidagdhīmiti strīpratyayena
saubhāgyātiśayapratīteḥ ।</p>

ṣoḍaśetyādisaṃkṣepaḥ । anenaivopāyena vicārya granthe pāṭho niśceyaḥ । sarveṣāṃ vṛttānāmityādāvarthaḥ

dvijottamāḥ'' ityadhyāyādau dṛśyate । <q>bhama</q>yoreva vyākhyātṛpāṭho vidyate । 2 <q>na</q>--etāni <q>bha</q>--eteṣu 3 <q>bha</q> N--pāde
4 <q>bha</q>--vṛttaṃ 4a--N vṛttā tanumadhyā ।। 5 <q>pa</q>--madhye laghunī cet vṛttaṃ tanumadhyā
‡ jādibānteṣvādarśeṣu ṣoḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ । N ādarśe'pi । asminnadhyāye vṛttalakṣaṇaṃ kāsucinmātṛkāsu
makārāditrikairevoktaṃ, anyāsu gurulaghuniyamena । pāṭhadvayasyāpi pāṭhāntarabhūyiṣṭhatvāt kevalaṃ saukaryāyobhayapāṭho'pi
mūlarūpeṇaiva mudritaḥ । piṅgalātpūrvaṃ chandolakṣaṇaṃ gurulaghusaṃkhyānenaiva vyavahṛtamiti dyotyate, na tu trikairiti ।
api cāsminnadhyāye kvacit vṛttajātyaiva lakṣaṇamuktaṃ, kvaciñcānuṣṭubhā । ayaṃ viśeṣo dhruvādhyāye'pi dṛśyate ।

nāma bhavati । yathā--bhātyaśokaḥ kisalayaḥ kusumastabakairamyaiḥ । śriyaṃ hastādharagatāṃ lajjayanniva ca strīṇām ।।"

tatra samastāsāṃ pañcabhedaḥ viṣamaścaturbhedaḥ ṣaṣṭho dvibhedaḥ dvitīye'rdhe tvekabhedaḥ, aṣṭamamekabhedam ।

<lg><l>āryāḥ śatasahasrāṇi jñeyā hyekannaviṃśatiḥ ।</l>

<p>adhyāyārthamupasaṃharan bhāvinaṃ viṣayamāsūtrayati vṛttairityādi । <q>kāvyavanthā</q> ityanenedamāha
yathā prāsādakuḍyādike kartavye prathamaṃ bhūmiḥ, tadvatkāvye nirmātavye bhūmikalpaḥ śabdacchandovidhiḥ
kṣetraparigrahaṃ vṛttasamāśrayamityādi viracayan bhittisthānīyaṃ lakṣaṇayojanaṃ
citrakarmapratimamalaṅkāraguṇaniveśanaṃ gavākṣavātāyanādideśīyo daśarūpakavibhāgaḥ upayoganirūpaṇāprakhyā
kākvādiplutiḥ evaṃbhūtavācanikābhinayasvarūpaṃ caturdaśādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhiradhyāyairucyate । tatrādhyāyadvayaṃ
vṛttalakṣaṇavidhānaṃ tu bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<p>yadyapi rūpakaviracanakāle paripakvaprajñasya na kramapratibhāsastathāpyapoddhāradhiyā kalpyata
ityāhuḥ । prabandhasya yo yukto'bhyāsaḥ tanniṣpattiḥ prabandhābhyāsaḥ tatsaṃpattiḥ abhinayārthanirvartanaṃ
tadabhinayopārohaṇamiti sa eva krama ityu<q>pādhyāyāḥ</q> । yadāhuḥ --

kramollaṅghane hi sati nāṭakādiviracayatāṃ mahāntaḥ pramādāpabhraṃśā bhavanti । na hi sarvo
<q>vālmīkirvyāsaḥ kālidāso bhaṭṭendurājo vā</q>, teṣāmapi
prāgjanmārjitakramābhyāsasamuditasaṃskārapāṭavotpāditaḥ kulapratibhaṅgajñānātiśaya iti śivam ।।</p>
<lg><l>iti pañcadaśādhyāye dhyāyinā parameśvaram ।</l>
<l>kṛtābhinavaguptena guptārthaprakaṭīkriyā ।।</l></lg>
<p>iti śrīmahāmāheśvarābhinavaguptācāryaviracitāyāṃ nāṭyaveda--
vivṛtāvabhinavabhāratyāṃ vṛttavidhirnāma
pañcaśo'dhyāyaḥ</p>

<pb n="294"/>

<p><q>śrīḥ</q></p>
<p><q>nāṭyaśāstram</q></p>
<p>ṣoḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ*</p>
<lg><l>†vibhūṣaṇaṃ cākṣarasaṃhatiśca śobhābhimānau guṇakīrtanaṃ ca ।</l>
<l>protsāhanodāharaṇe niruktaṃ guṇānuvādo'tiśayaḥ sahetuḥ ।। 1</l></lg>
<lg><l>sārūpyamithyādhyavasāyasiddhi--
padoccayākrandamanorathāśca ।</l>
<l>ākhyānayāñcāpratiṣedhapṛcchā--
dṛṣṭāntanirbhāsanasaṃśayāśca ।। 2</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 294 !-->
<lg><l>vicitraṃ rūpakabhuvo lakṣaṇaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ bhuvaḥ ।</l>
<l>bhāsyate yena taṃ vande prācyadhīsādhitaṃ śivam ।।</l></lg>
<p>(nanu) kāvyabandhāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇānvitāḥ kartavyā ityuktaṃ, tatra guṇālaṅkārādi--
ri( ?dīrī)ti vṛttayaśceti kāvyeṣu prasiddho mārgaḥ, lakṣaṇāni tu na prasiddhāni, kiṃ ca
puruṣasyeva kāvyasya lakṣaṇaguṇālaṅkāravyavahāro na yuktaḥ puruṣasya śarīra--
caitanyabhedāt kaṭakādīnāṃ tato'pi bhedāt, kāvyasya punarviracanakāle prati--
<!-- APPARATUS page 294 !-->
*<q>jātibā</q>nteṣu saptadaśo'dhyāyaḥ ।
†asminnadhyāye ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇasamuddeśānirdeśayorguṇadaśakasya lakṣaṇe ca dvividhaḥ pāṭho dṛśyate ।
tatra vṛttikāreṇaikaḥ pāṭho gṛhītaḥ, kīrtidharadhanañjayasarveśvarādibhiśca sa eva pramāṇīkṛtaḥ । bhinnaḥ
pāṭhaścirantanaiḥ kaiścidvyākhyātṛbhiḥ paṭhitaḥ, sa tu viśvanāthasiṅgabhūpālādibhiranusṛtaḥ । vṛttikārasteṣāṃ
vaiṣamyapariharaṇāya nāmanirvacanayorbhinnānāmapi keṣāṃcillakṣaṇānāṃ svapāṭhoktalakṣaṇeṣvantarbhāvaṃ prakaṭīkṛtya
ṣaṭtriṃśattvaṃ samyagasthāpayat । bhojadevastūbhayoḥ pāṭhayoḥ samānāni bhinnāni ca gṛhītvānyāni
dvādaśa saṃkalayya catuḥ ṣaṣṭilakṣaṇāni nāmanirvacanābhyāṃ prāpañcayat । tanmatameva śāradātanayenānu--

<pb n="295"/>

<lg><l>āśīḥ priyoktiḥ 1kapaṭaḥ kṣamā ca
prāptiśca paścāttapanaṃ tathaiva2 ।</l></lg>
<lg><l>3arthānuvṛttirhyupapattiyuktī</l>
<l>kāryoṃ'nunītiḥ paridevanaṃ ca ।। 3</l></lg>
<lg><l>ṣaṭtriṃśadetāni 4tu lakṣaṇāni</l>
<l>proktāni vai bhūṣaṇasaṃmitāni ।</l>
<l>kāvyeṣu 5bhāvārthagatāni tajjñaiḥ</l>
<l>samyakprayojyāni yathārasaṃ tu6 ।। 4</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 295 !-->
pattikāle vā prāpakasattāyāṃ teṣāmagaṇitatvācca । daṇḍināpi
"kāvyaśobhākarāndharmānalaṅkārānpracakṣate"
iti bruvatā guṇamadhya eva tatra prasādādīnabhidadhatā ca guṇālaṅkāravibhāgo'pyasaṃbhavīti sūcitaṃ
bhavati । satyametat, kiṃ tu viracanavivecanasāmarthyasamarthanāyāvaśyaṃ kālpaniko'pi vibhāga
āśrayaṇīyaḥ । tatra kalpanāyāṃ vipratipattayaḥ kecidāhuḥ --iha guṇāstāvadātmani cinmaye
śṛṅgārādau vartante, śṛṅgāre cāvaśyaṃ ca lakṣyata iti pṛthaksiddhatvādalaṅkāraḥ, śarīraniṣṭhameva yatpadaṃ
pṛthaksiddhaṃ tallakṣaṇam, yena śarīrasya saundaryaṃ jāyate । tacca siddharūpaṃ sādhyarūpaṃ vā, yathā
śyāmeti, 'madamantharagāminī' iti ca । etadeva lakṣaṇaṃ, taccālaṅkriyate । alaṅkārairyuktaṃ kāvyaṃ
lakṣaṇairvinā na śobhate । kriyāvācyopameyabhedena tadetallakṣaṇaṃ dvidheti yathā 'śyāmā viśālākṣī'
'mattamātaṅgagāminī' iti ca ।</p>
<p>anye manyante --itivṛttakhaṇḍa[la]kānyeva sandhyaṅgakāni lakṣaṇānīti ca vyapadiśyante ।
nimittabhedāt pūrvāparasaṃbandhena bījopakṣipte'rthe nirvahaṇaparyante
<!-- APPARATUS page 295 !-->
1 <q>bha</q>-- kapaṭakṣame 2 <q>bha</q>--grahaśca 3 <q>bha</q>--arthānuvṛttī upapatti 4 <q>bha</q>--mayā samāsāt 5 <q>bha</q>--sodāharaṇeṣu 6 <q>bha</q>--
rasāni ।
sṛtam । ataḥ prathamaṃ vṛttikārapāṭhavilasitamadhyāyaṃ samāpyānubandharūpeṇa pāṭhāntarabhāgo nirvacanodāharaṇasahito
mahāmatīnāṃ cittavilāsoddyotanāya sūkṣmaviṣayavivecanalālasānāṃ hitāya ca saṃprayojito'dhyāyānte
yathālabdhagranthaparikaraḥ ।

<pb n="296"/>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 296 !-->
parasparasandhāyakatvena sandhyaṅgatayā vyapadeśaḥ, rasaviśeṣopayogitayā vṛttyaṅgavācoyuktiḥ,
kāvyagatakhyātiprāśastyopayogitayā mahāpuruṣagatapāśadhvajapādarekhādivallakṣaṇaśabdavācyatā । taduktaṃ
tatreva--</p>
<lg><l>lakṣaṇānyeva bījārthakramanirvāhakāni ca । iti,</l>
<l>pratisandhitadaṅgāni phalasiddhyupapattitaḥ ।। iti ।</l></lg>
<p>(kavye dhīrodāttādiguṇādhānaṃ vastuvarṇanābhaṅgirveti kecit) tadatra prathamapakṣe
varṇanīyapradhānabhūtādhikārapuruṣagataguṇādivibhāga eva kāvye paryavasīyate । dvitīyapakṣe tu varṇanīyaḥ
sakala eva* itivṛttalakṣaṇo'rthaḥ kāvyabhedāt tredhā vibhajyate । ekeṣāṃ tu darśanaṃ --kaveryaḥ
pratibhātmā prathamaparispandaḥ tadvyāpārabalopanatā guṇāḥ, pratibhāvata eva hi rasābhivyañjanasāmarthyaṃ
mādhuryāderupanibandhanasāmarthyaṃ, na sāmānyakaveḥ । anena śabdenedaṃ vastu
varṇayāmītyevaṃbhūtavarṇanāparaparyāyādvitīyavyāpārasaṃpādyāstvalaṅkārāḥ ।</p>
<p>śabdānamībhiḥ śabdairarthānamībhirarthaiḥ saṃghaṭayāmītyevamātmakastu yastṛtīyaḥ kaveḥ parispandaḥ
tadadhīnātmalābhādiśabdātmārthātmakakāvyaśarīrasaṃśritāni vakṣyamāṇaśleṣādiguṇa--
daśakasamabhivyañjanavyāpārāṇi śabdārthopasaṃskārakalpāni kriyārūpāṇi lakṣaṇānīti, yaduktaṃ
tatraiva--
<lg><l>iti śabdārthayoryeyaṃ saṃśritā dehabhūtayoḥ ।</l>
<l>kāvye tayā darśitāni lakṣaṇāni (vidurbudhāḥ) ।। iti,</l></lg>
<lg><l>kāvye'pyasti tathā kaścit snigdhaḥ sparśo'rthaśabdayoḥ ।</l>
<l>yaḥ śleṣādiguṇavyaktidakṣaḥ syāllakṣaṇasthitaḥ ।। iti,</l></lg>
<lg><l>ceṣṭālaṅkāradṛṣṭāntacihnaṃ.......... ।। iti ca</l></lg>
atra pakṣe kavivyāpārabhedādguṇālaṅkāralakṣaṇavibhāgaḥ ।</p>
<p>apare saṃgirante--abhineyānāṃ kāvyabandhānāṃ vakṣyamāṇasvarūpaṃ ca rūpakaṃ samabhidadhyāt,
kaveḥ svasāmarthyādhānāya tāvadabhyāso nirmāṇavidheyo lakṣaṇaṃ, mastakāsaṃpūrṇaścādau krameṇa tu
tathābhūto'bhineyārthaḥ kāvyabandho(lakṣaṇonnītaḥ) tena ca lokottarahṛdyavarṇane yogāt । tathā hi
kiñcit prabandhajātaṃ guṇālaṅkāranikarapradhānaṃ yathā <q>meghadūtākhyaṃ</q> tadvibhūṣaṇam evamanyadapīti ।</p>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 297 !-->
miti1 । pare tvabhāṣanta ( ?tvābhāṣante)--alaṅkārādinirapekṣeṇaiva( ?nirapekṣayaiva) nisargasundaro
yo'bhine(na) yaviśeṣaḥ kāvyeṣu dṛśyate, <q>amaruka</q>ślokeṣvapi(? ṣviva), tatsaundaryaheturyo dharmaḥ
sa lakṣaṇaṃ2 sa eva cārthaḥ kāvyaśarīraviśeṣarūpo lakṣaṇam । upamā--dipaka--rūpakāṇām
ānantyād ( ?ānantyaprayojakatvād)bhedamāhuḥ । tuśabdena* ( ?śabdena) arthena citratvaṃ lakṣaṇamityanye ।</p>
<p>itareṣāṃ tu mataṃ yathāṃ tantraprasaṅgabādhātideśādi mīmāṃsāprasiddhaṃ vākyaviśeṣavyavacchedalakṣaṇaṃ
tathā kāvyaviśeṣavyavacchedakaṃ bhūṣaṇādilakṣaṇajātamiti tvayaṃ pakṣo dvitīyapakṣānna bhidyate ।
eteṣu tu pakṣeṣvanyatamagrahe viśeṣaṇāni na saṃgacchante spaṣṭena pathā । adaṃ tu daśapakṣyāṃ vastu ।</p>
<p>iha kāvyārthā rasā ityuktaṃ prāk । uktaṃ ca varṇanīyaṃ śabdanīyaṃ kaveḥ karmeti ca
vyutpattitrayaṃ kāvyamiti । anenābhidheyaṃ abhidhānaṃ abhidhāṃ ca svīkṛtyāvasthīyate, api ca
śabdavyāpāro'bhidhātṛvyāpāraḥ pratipādyavyāpāraśceti trigataḥ । tatra śabdasya
rasābhivyaktikṣamārthapratipādakatvaṃ svayaṃ ca śrotre ca saṃkrantimātraṃ nāntarīyakatayā
tadrasadarśanayogyatāpādanasāmarthyādguṇaśabdavācyam । āvartamāno dvitīyo varṇaḥ padaṃ vā
prāktanavarṇanādaśobhāheturalaṅkāraḥ । evamarthasyāpi, yadrasābhivyaktihetutvaṃ so'rthaguṇaḥ yastu
vastvantaraṃ vandanasyeva candraḥ so'laṅkāraḥ, yastu trividho'pyabhidhāvyāpāraḥ sa lakṣaṇānāṃ
viṣayaḥ । tathāhi-- idamanena śabdenānayetikartavyatayā'munāśayenetthaṃbhūtabuddhijananāya bruve iti
kaviḥ pravartate, sa tathābhūtaṃ rasavatkāvyaṃ vidhatte । tatra cittavṛttyātmakaṃ rasaṃ
lakṣayaṃstattadrasocitavibhāvādvaicitryasampādakastrividho'bhidhāvyāpāro lakṣaṇaśabdenocyate । ityeṣāṃ
sāmānyalakṣaṇam । yathā ca pīvaratvaṃ stanayorlakṣaṇaṃ madhyasya tu kulakṣaṇaṃ, evaṃ kiñcidabhidhīyamānaṃ
kenacidrūpeṇa rasocitena vibhāvādirūpeṇa tameva padārthakramaṃ lakṣayallakṣaṇaṃ anyatra tu tatkulakṣaṇaṃ,
tena sarve'laṅkārā 3guṇāśca tatsamudāyādvilakṣaṇā bhavanti । tathā svārtho'pi ca kvacidarthamātraṃ
kvacidalaṅkāro'rthataḥ kvāpi citrataḥ kvacidalaṅkārādiprakriyāvihīno'pi svayaṃ sundarasvabhāvo'rthaḥ
kutracicchanda iti trividhavyāpāragāmī; taddvāreṇābhidhānābhidheyatadguṇālaṅkārādyanugrahaḥ śabdānāṃ
śabdairarthānāmarthaiḥ śabdānāmarthaistathāparaiḥ saṃghaṭanāṃ vicitrāṃ kārayamāṇābhidhāvyāpāravatī
hyuktirnirvāṇapradhānadhurādhirohī lakṣaṇākhya eva ।</p>

<pb n="298"/>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 298 !-->
<p>ata eva pūrvaṃ "kāvyabandhāstu kartavyāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇānvitāḥ" (nā.śā.15/227)iti
lakṣaṇānyeva hi pradhānaṃ tatprasaṅgena guṇālaṅkārā iti tātparyam । viśeṣalakṣaṇavyākhyāne
caitatsphoṭayiṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>tatra lakṣaṇānyuddeṣṭuṃ tāvadāha <q>vibhūṣaṇa</q>mityādi <q>yathārasaṃ</q> tvityantena ślokacatuṣṭyena ।
yathārasaṃ ye bhāvā vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicāriṇaḥ, teṣāṃ yo'rthaḥ (taṃ) sthāyibhāvarasīkaraṇātmakaṃ
prayojanāntaraṃ gatāni prāptāni, yadabhidhāvyāpāropasaṃkrāntā udyānādayo'rthāstadrasaviśeṣavibhāvādibhāvaṃ
pratipadyante tāni lakṣaṇānīti sāmānyalakṣaṇam । ata eva kāvye samyakprayojyānīti
viṣayasteṣāmuktaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>bhaṭṭanāyakenāpi</q> (kuśalaśikṣitā)*bhidhāvyāpārapradhānaṃ kāvyamityuktaṃ --</p>
<lg><l>śabdaprādhānyamāśritya tatra śāstraṃ pṛthagviduḥ ।</l>
<l>arthe tattvena yukte tu vajantyākhyānametayoḥ ।</l>
<l>dvayorguṇatve vyāpāraprādhānye kāvyagīrbhavet ।। iti ।</l></lg>
bhāmahenāpi--
<p>"saiṣā sarvaiva vaktoktiranayārtho vibhāvyate" (2--75) ityādi । tena ca paramārthe vyāpāra
eva lakṣaṇaṃ, sa tu viṣayadvāreṇa viśeṣalakṣaṇe tu nirūpyata iti tatsvīkṛtatvādartho'pi lakṣaṇaṃ,
vyāpāro'pi ca tadvidāṃ tu tadabhyāsaparāṇāṃ ca tathābhūtakāvyātmakaviṣayāvalokane jhaṭityeva
pratibhāti । tadanyatrānumānena pratibhayā svasaṃvedanā--ityanena prayojanam । kuśalaśikṣitavyāpāro
hi tatkāvyadṛśi bhātyeva ।</p>
<p><q>ṣaṭtriṃśaditi</q> ca nānyaditi vāraṇaparaṃ kavihṛdayavartināmaparāṇāmaparisaṃkhyeyatvāt । kiṃ tu
bāhulyena tāvadiyatā lakṣyavyāptaṃ, iyati ca kavināvadhātavyamiti saṃkhyānirūpaṇam ।</p>
<p>tathā ca matāntareṇa bharatamunirevānyathāpyuddeśalakṣaṇena nāmāntarairapi ca vyavahāraṃ karoti;
tata eva pustakeṣu bhedo dṛśyate taṃ ca darśayiṣyāmaḥ। paṭhitoddeśakramastvasmadupādhyāya-
paramparāgataḥ ।।</p>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 299 !-->
<p>tatra vibhūṣaṇaṃ lakṣayitumāha <q>alaṅkārai</q>riti । bhūṣaṇaiḥ kaṭakādibhiḥ vibhajya
sthānadeśakāladaśāpuruṣādivibhāgaṃ vicārya nyastairiva guṇālaṅkārairyadalaṅkaraṇaṃ tadbhūṣaṇaṃ nāma lakṣaṇaṃ
kavivyāpāraḥ, taddvāreṇa śabdārthavyāpārāvapi ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati--iha guṇā alaṅkārāśca viṣayā ityanena nibaddhāḥ kāvyārthīkṛtānāmabhidheyānāṃ
rasaviśeṣaviṣayaṃ vibhāvādibhāvaṃ vivarītuṃ samarthāḥ । tathā hi hāsyarasapradhāne prahasanādau
śuṣkaśrotriye vaktari prayoktari śrotari vā guṇaviniveśitaṃ tu lakṣaṇaṃ bhajatyalaṅkāraśca । tathā hi
pādatāḍitake* śrotriyaṃ śrotāramabhipretya viṭasyāpi nirguṇapuruṣasyaivoktiḥ "mā musalenāpākārṣīḥ,
mā kusū( ?kū)lāgninā dhākṣīḥ" iti śobhāṃ puṣṇāti । anaucityanibandhastu karuṇavipralambhādau
yamakasya yathā--
<lg><l>vinā priyatamenādya virahānalatāpitā ।</l>
<l>dahyeccūtasya vicchedaṃ kiṃ tu hā nalatāpitā ।।</l></lg>
sthāne niveśastu yathā--
<lg><l>līneva pratibimbiteva likhitevāntarnikhāteva ca
protkīrṇeva ca vajralepaghaṭiteva" iti । (mālatīmādhava 5/10)</l></lg>
atrāpi loke utprekṣāparamparaiva hīyaṃ sātiśayakāmāveśāvasthāsamuddyotita--
priyatamāviṣayavicitrasaṃkalpagarbhasaṃbhavaunmukhyaprāṇatvād vipralambhasya kāmāvasthānāṃ ca
mādhuryaprasādopete ca kāvye śrotrapathamavataratyeveti pratipādyate ।
sukumāracittavṛttisubhago'yamuttamaścetyevaṃ samastasya guṇālaṅkāravargasyānugrāhakamidaṃ kavivyāpārarūpaṃ,
tadvaśācca śabdārthatadvyāpārādyapi spṛśadvibhūṣaṇākhyaṃ lakṣaṇam । etamevārthaṃ samyagānandavardhanācāryo'pi
vivicya nyarūpayat--
<lg><l>dhvanyātmabhūte śṛṅgāre samīkṣya viniveśitaḥ ।</l>

<lg><l>1yatrālpairakṣaraiḥ śliṣṭairvicitrārthopavarṇanam2 ।</l>
<l>tadapyakṣarasaṅghātaṃ vidyāllakṣaṇasaṃjñitam ।। 6</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 300 !-->
ityuktvā krameṇa--
<lg><l>vivakṣā tatparatvena nāṅgitvena kadācana ।</l>
<l>kāle ca grahaṇatyāgau nātinirvahaṇaiṣitā ।।</l></lg> (dhvanyāloke--2--18)ityādinā
granthasandarbheṇa sodāharaṇena । taccāsmābhiḥ <q>sahṛdayālokalocane</q> tadvivaraṇe vistarato vyākhyātamiti
tatkutūhalantadeva gṛhṇīyāt । iha tu prasaktyā granthabhūyastvādudvijate loka iti na
vistāritam ।।</p>
<p>athākṣarasaṃhatimāha <q>yatrālpai</q>riti । akṣaraśabdena yadṛcchāśabdaprādhānyaṃ, yadṛcchāśabdeṣu
svarūpasyaiva pravṛttinimittatvāt tenālpairevākṣaraiḥ śliṣṭairviprakṛtāvityuktābhirupalakṣitatvenaiva vicitraṃ
tadrasocitavibhāvādibhāvaṃ prāpyamāṇo'rtha upavarṇyate, śrotṝṇāṃ hṛdayamupasaṃkrāmayituṃ yattasmin
kavivyāpāro'kṣarasaṅghātastatkāraṇatvāt ।</p>
<p>tathāhi māninītyakṣarāṇi īrṣyāvipralambhe, taruṇītyābhilāṣike, varatanuriti saṃbhoge vibhāvatāṃ
tāmeva prāpayanti । astītivyutpattistathāpi paryante mānādiśabdānāmantato vā dhātupratyayamātrāderavaśyaṃ
yadṛcchātvamityakṣarāṇāmeva saṃghātaḥ pradhāna yadṛcchāśabdaprādhānye udāharaṇaṃ yathā--
<lg><l>*visrambhāduttamāṅgaṃ plavagabalapateḥ pādamakṣasya hantuḥ
kṛtvotsaṅge salīlaṃ tvaci kanakamṛgasyāṅgamādhāya śeṣam ।</l>
<l>bāṇaṃ rakṣaḥkulaghnaṃ praguṇitamanujenādarāttī'kṣṇamakṣṇoḥ
koṇenodvīkṣamāṇastvadanujavadane dattakarṇo'yamāste ।।</l></lg>
visrambhādityādīnāṃ maitrīpradhānavālihananapūrvakasāmrājyadātṛtvabalāccetyuktam ।
akṣasya yo hantetyekākināpi yenāśokavanikāviploṣaṇaṃ rākṣasabalakṣapaṇaṃ ca
kṛtaṃ, so'pi yatra pradhānaprakṛtirbhavatītyuktam । tvacīti prahatamārīcavṛttāntaḥ ।
bāṇamityādinā tatraivāsya bahumāna ityuktam । rākṣasaviṣayadaivavaiguṇyamityuktam ।

<lg><l>siddhairarthaiḥ samaṃ kṛtvā 1hyasiddho'rthaḥ prasādhyate ।</l>
<l>2yatra ślakṣṇā vicitrārthā sā śobhetyābhisaṃjñitā3 ।। 7</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 301 !-->
atra ca yatra yasya yadvyāpārastatra prādhānyasya kā katheti । praguṇitamiti bahutararaṇasaṃmardadhurandharatayā
kuṭilīkṛtasyāpi kṣetrabahumāne punaryojanam । <q>tvadanujavadana</q> iti bhedopāyakṛtā nitisaṃpat parapakṣe
ca viparyayam । <q>dattakarṇa</q> iti tadākarṇanamātrametat, na tu hṛdaye nirvyājaṃ tejojājvalyamānaujasi
bhedaṃ prati ko'pyasya bahumānaḥ । <q>aya</q>miti gambhīradhīrākṛtiḥ pratyāsannaścāsta iti । yadyapi
prakṛte nāpi kaścitkṣobho'ta evoktaṃ salīlamiti। atra cārthasyālaṅkāraghaṭanāprayāsamantareṇaiva
sundaratvaṃ lakṣaṇakṛtameva ।</p>
<p>nanu sābhiprāyamātratvaṃ nāmārthasya tu guṇa oja ityuktam* । śobhāḥ sahṛdayāḥ artho
jaḍastasyābhiprāya iti kathaṃ, bhāṣāvaktṛśrotroḥ sa iti cet tadgato'rthasya guṇa iti katham ।</p>
<p>atha vastvantarākṣepakatvameva tasya sa guṇa ityucyate tadvastvantaramākṣipyaṃ
vaktrabhiprāyarūpamevākṣepakatvamapi kavimanīṣāvyāpārabalādeva tathāviniveśanāt, prakārāyoge
tathābhāvāt । ata eva prauḍhirvastuto vaktṛgataiva natvarthe kāmamupacaryatāmityalaṃ bahunā ।</p>
<p>eteṣāṃ ca lakṣaṇānāṃ saṃkīrṇatvena lakṣyaṃ dṛśyate bāhulyāpekṣayā tūdāharaṇaṃ mantavyam ।
atha śobhā-siddhairarthairīti । yathā--
medaśchedakṛśodaraṃ laghubhavatyutthānayogyaṃ vapuḥ
sattvānāmapi lakṣyate vikṛtimaccittaṃ bhayakrodhayoḥ ।
utkarṣaḥ sa ca dhanvināṃ yadiṣavaḥ sidhyanti lakṣye cale
mithyā hi vyasanaṃ vadanti mṛgayāmīdṛgvinodaḥ kutaḥ । (śāku 2.5)</p>

samavikalaṃ mṛgayālakṣaṇamarthaṃ kṛtvā aprasiddho'nucito'pi so'rtha ucito
vicitraśca nirupitaḥ । na cātrālaṅkāraḥ kaściditi kavivyāpāreṇa yaḥ

<p>athābhimānaḥ--<q>dhāryamāṇastu bahubhi</q>riti । yathā mamaiva--

atra hi tādṛśyarthasyārthena ghaṭanā kṛtā yasyāṃ kāryayuktibhiḥ phalayojanābhirdhāryamāṇo hṛdaye

tathābhūto'rtho'laukikatvāttāvānupāyaḥ kavinālaṅkāra upamānopameyabhāvasya
kathaṃcidapyasvikārātkevalaṃ vakturabhimataṃ vadatā kimiva mayāpyevaṃ tadapi
naivetyabhidhānamabhidhānākhyalakṣaṇam । etadeva sādṛśyanāmnāpyanyairuktam ।

amṛtakaratvaṃ hi candrasya śrutaṃ kālakūṭasahodaratvaṃ ca, mantrāṇāṃ viṣaśamanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ, svayamanubhūtaṃ
mohādi tatsamudbhavaṃ yatprakṛte sādṛśyaṃ tena lokadṛṣṭena tulyavṛttāntatvaṃ tatkṣobhaṃ hṛdaye'navasthānaṃ
janayati--yadyamṛtasadṛśaścandrapādāḥ tatkimevamaṅgaṃ vidadhyuriti( ?) । evamanyat ।</p>

ayaṃ spaṣṭārthaḥ ।</p>

ca bhavān murārirityādi । idamanyatra priyavacanamiti paṭhitam --

<lg><l>niruktaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ 1tathyaṃ cātathyameva ca ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 304 !-->
<lg><l>sarvaṃ sādhvathavā ruṇatsi virahakṣāmasya rāmasya cet</l>
<l>tvaddantāṅkitavālipa(ka?)kṣarudhiraklinnāgrapuṅkhaṃ śaram ।।</l></lg>
<p>atra hi rāvaṇīyadaśitiparighaṭṭita(vālikakṣa)pāṭane udāhṛte sa svāvamāno'rthe'vagate sati
tadapajayaḥ tatkakṣakṣayyaparigrahastathaiva caturarṇavabhramaṇaṃ punaḥ kṛpāmātreṇa tyāgaḥ tatrāpratīkāraḥ
punarabhimāno darpa ityādi gamyate । akṣarasaṃhateśca viśeṣaḥ --tatrāvayopādātavyaśabdāntarasthāne
śabdāntaropādānaṃ hanumata iti vaktavye'kṣasya hanturiti, iha tu tvaddanteti
tadīyādhikārodāharaṇam । anye paṭhanti --
<lg><l>yatra tulyārthayuktena vākyenābhipradarśanāt ।</l>
<l>sādhyante nipuṇairarthāstadudāharaṇaṃ smṛtam ।। iti ।</l></lg>
tulyairarthaistatsamayabhāvibhiryaduktaṃ yadvākyamiti sa eva phalato'rthaḥ ।।</p>
<p>atha niruktaṃ --<q>niruktaṃ dvividha</q>miti । siddhirlakṣaṇena svikāraḥ । tayā prasādhitaṃ
tathyaṃ, tato'nyadatathyam । udāharaṇaṃ yathā mamaiva--
<lg><l>vīrotsave saṅgarasīmni mūḍhaṃ yaḥ prāpayat satyapathaṃ kathaṃcit ।</l>
<l>satyārjunaḥ so'pi ca nāma kṛṣṇaḥ prasiddhiritthaṃ vitathaiva sarvā ।।</l></lg>
parasparaṃ nāmnoranyatra tathyatvaṃ svaviṣaye tvatathyateti । na cāyamarthaḥ śleṣaḥ, sa hi tulyasaṃkhyayoḥ ।
yathā "gāvo vaḥ pāvanānāṃ" *iti gośabdasya raśmiṣu surabhiṣu cānāditvena prasiddheḥ । iha
tvekatrānyatve kṛtaḥ samaya iti । evaṃ pṛthaktathyātathyayorudāhāryam । anyatra pāṭhaḥ --

1 <q>bha</q>--yaṃ 2 <q>ca</q>--siddhiprasādhitaṃ 3 <q>bha</q>--cāpyasādhakam ।
*saṃpūrṇaḥ ślokaḥ--
dattānandāḥ prajānāṃ samucitasamayākliṣṭa sṛṣṭaiḥ payobhiḥ
pūrvāhṇe viprakīrṇā diśi diśi viramatyahni saṃhārabhājaḥ ।
dīptāṃśordīrghaduḥkhaprabhavabhavabhayodanvaduttāranāvo

<lg><l>1guṇānuvādo hīnānāmuttamairupamākṛtaḥ ।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 305 !-->
<lg><l>niravadyasya vākyasya pūrvoktārthaprasiddhaye ।</l>
<l>yaducyate tu vacanaṃ niruktaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।।</l></lg>
pūrvaṃ yatprokto bāhyasya saṃbandhī kaścidarthastasya prasiddhaye'vadyabhāvasya vācakaṃ yaducyate tena
niruktamiti nirarthakamevātra vācyam । yathā--satyaṃ *sa rājāprakṛtirañjanāditi ।</p>
<p>atha guṇānuvādaḥ-- guṇānuvāda iti parimitasyāpāditotkṛṣṭaguṇanayopamā, tatkṛto
guṇānāmutsekaḥ । yathā --
<lg><l>pālitā dyaurivendreṇa tvayā rājanvasundharā ।।</l></lg>
nanūpameyamalaṅkāraḥ, kimataḥ, uktaṃ hyalaṅkārāṇāṃ vaicitryaṃ lakṣaṇakṛtameva । eta eva śikṣitairāpi
<q>daṇḍiprabhṛti</q>bhirye nirupitā upamābhedāḥ, tatra yo bhedako'śaḥ ācikhyāsāsaṃśrayanirṇayādirarthaḥ, sa
tādṛkpṛthagalaṅkāratayā gaṇitaḥ। gaṇane'pi vā saṃsṛṣṭisaṅkarāpattiḥ । arthamātraṃ taditi cet tarhi
tadeva lakṣaṇam । yathā hi rājatā vibhajya vicāryamāṇā itthamavatiṣṭhate--makuṭādyalaṅkāraḥ
śauryādiguṇo vyūḍhoraskatvādilakṣaṇasamudāyo rājālaṅkāryaśca guṇavāṃśca lakṣaṇīyaśca, tathā kāvyamapi
tena guṇālaṅkāravyatiriktāḥ sarve lakṣaṇamiti mantavyam । "astyuttarasyāṃ* "iti hi pūrvārdhe
ākhyānaṃ nāma lakṣaṇam । nanvevaṃ sarvatra lakṣaṇayogaḥ, ka ākṣepārthaḥ priyamevāsmākamadaḥ
tatsarvamalaṅkārayuktaṃ kāvyam । nanu gaurvāhīka iti rūpakayoge'pi, kiṃ na kāvyam ?
doṣaparivarjanaguṇavattva--rasavattvādivaikalyāditi cet, asmāsvāpādito doṣastvayaivonmūlita
ityāstām ।</p>
<p>anyatra tu pāṭhaḥ--

*astyuttarasyāṃ diśi devatātmā himālayo nāma nagādhirājaḥ ।

<l>prārabdhaṃ parato† yathā manasijasyecchā tathā vartituṃ</l>
<l>premṇā maugdhyavibhūṣitasya sahajaḥ ko'pyeṣa kāntaḥ kramaḥ ।।</l></lg>
atrerṣyātmā yaḥ premaṇyuttame'rthastato'pi viśeṣa uktaḥ । pratipadaṃ cābhiprāyo'sti sa vivecanīyaḥ।।
na ceyamatiśayoktiḥ saṃbhāvyamānatvāt । so'pi vā lakṣaṇenālaṅkāra iti vakṣyāmaḥ samanantarameva।
anyatra tu paṭhyate--
<lg><l>bahūn guṇān kīrtayitvā sāmānyajanasaṃbhavān ।</l>
<l>viśeṣaḥ kīrtyate yatra jñeyaḥ so'tiśayo budhaiḥ ।। iti ।</l></lg>
atha sa hetuḥ--bahūnāṃ <q>bhāṣamāṇānāmiti</q> । bahūn bhāṣamāṇānanādṛtyaikasyāsādhāraṇasyārthasya nirṇayaḥ
kartavyatvenāvalambya siddhasya pramāṇopamānavacanamupakṣepavacanaṃ mama tāvadevaṃ pratibhāsate iti
sahetuḥ । yathā <q>bhaṭṭendurājasya</q>--
<lg><l>eke vārinidhipraveśamapare lokāntarālokanaṃ</l>
<l>kecitpāvakayoginaṃ nijagaduḥ kṣīṇe'hni candrārciṣām ।</l>
<l>mithyā caitadasākṣikaṃ priyasakhi pratyakṣatīvrātapo</l>
<l>manye'haṃ punaradhvanīnaramaṇīceto'dhiśete raviḥ ।।</l></lg>
<!-- APPARATUS page 306 !-->
1 <q>ca</q>-- uttamārthaviśiṣṭo 2 <q>bha</q>-- viśeṣo yaḥ 3 <q>ba</q>--anekārthaviniścayaḥ <q>ca</q>-- anekārthavinirṇayāt ।
* dvayorapyabhinavabhāratīmātṛkayorayaṃ śloko bhaṭṭendurājasyeti vartate । ayamamarukakāvye dṛśyate
vyākhyātaścārjunavarmavemabhūpālābhyām । vṛttikāravacanaprāmāṇyādayamamaruke prakṣipta iti saṃbhāvyate ।
† prārabdhāparato -- Kavi; prārabdhaṃ parato--<q>madhusūdanī</q>

<lg><l>siddhopamānavacanaṃ heturityabhisaṃjñitaḥ ।। 14</l></lg>
<lg><l>1apadeśastu parokṣo yasmādutpadyate'nukaraṇena ।</l>

<lg><l>4abhūtapūrvairyatrārthaistattulyārthasya nirṇayaḥ ।</l></lg>

(ekasyeti) ekamasādhāraṇam । (<q>siddhopamāneti</q>) ḍumiñ prakṣepaṇe ityasyopamānam । anyatra

<lg><l>yatprayojanasāmarthyādvākyaṃ śiṣṭārthasādhanam ।</l>

samyagasyate hṛdi kṣipyate yena sa samāsaḥ upapattistayoktā ।

<lg><l>saindūrīkṛtasāndrakuṅkumarasapracchāyamālocyate</l>

<l>tattejo jaraṭhāṃśutāṃ kalayatā bhāvipravāsāvadhiṃ</l>
<l>sandhyāmugdhavadhūkapolaphalake kīrṇo nakhāgrāṅkuraḥ ।।</l></lg>
atra yaditi nirdeśyaṃ parokṣavastu tattvasyāparijñānāt । anukaraṇena pracchāyamātreṇa,
apadeśyamālocyamiti lakṣaṇena saindūrīkṛtetyādinā । samānaṃ sapramāṇakaṃ karaṇaṃ darśanakriyā
yasya tādṛśe vastuni sārūpyaṃ lakṣaṇam । paurṇamāsyāmapi vakrarekhevendorbhāgo lakṣyate
udayācalāntaritatvāt sandhyāsamaye । na ceyamupamā upameyasyābhāvādupameyameva hi pūrvārdhena
liṃgyate । pustakāntareṣu tu pāṭhaḥ--
<lg><l>yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ yathārūpaṃ ca varṇyate ।</l>
<l>yatpratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā dṛṣṭaṃ tadvarṇato'pi ca ।। iti ।</l></lg></p>
<p>pratyakṣaṃ vastu parokṣamiva deśakālarūpānusāreṇa varṇyate ।</p>
<p>atha mithyādhyavasāyaḥ-- <q>abhūtapūrvairyatrā</q>rthairiti । apāramārthikairevārthai--

<p>atha manorathaḥ-- <q>hṛdayasthasya</q> bhāvasyeti । yathā--

nirgaṇḍa durārohāṃ mā putraka pāṭalīṃ samāroha ।
ārūḍhanipatitā ke'nayā na kṛtā iha grāme ।।

<lg><l>anekayukti yadvākyamanekārthaprasādhakam1 ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 313 !-->
yadayamityādi kasya hetorhālāhalakālakūṭakavalanādinā yena sāmyaṃ kṛtaṃ sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ । na
ceyamupamā, yato nidarśanena pratyakṣīkaraṇāya kṛta ita idamevaṃ kartumudyata iti, na ca rūpakaṃ
yadetatkaroti tata idamasya bhaviṣyatīti bhinnakālatvāt, tadāha pūrvopalabdhau satyāmiti ।</p>
<p>atha bhāsanaṃ--<q>anekayukti yadvākyamiti</q> । yathā--
"kartā dyūtacchalānāṃ jatumayaśaraṇoddīpanaḥ so'bhimānī" * (veṇī)--ityādi । bhāsyate prakṛtaḥ
krodhādiryena । pāṭhāntaraṃ--</p>
<lg><l>īpsitārthaprasiddhyarthaṃ kīrtyante yatra sūribhiḥ ।</l>
<l>prayojanānyanekāni sā māletyabhisaṃjñitā ।। iti</l></lg>
<p>atha saṃśayaḥ-- <q>aparijñātatattvārtha</q>mityādi । yathā--
<lg><l>tiṣṭhetkopavaśātprabhāvapihitā dīrghaṃ na sā kupyati</l>
<l>svargāyotpatitā bhavenmayi punarbhāvārdramasyā manaḥ ।</l>
<l>tāṃ hartuṃ vibudhadviṣo'pi na ca me śaktāḥ purovartinīṃ</l>
<l>sā cātyantamagocaraṃ nayanayoryāteti ko'yaṃ vidhiḥ ।।</l></lg>
(vikramo. 4--2)
atrādyo bhāgaḥ saṃśayodāharaṇaṃ, anantarastūpapattyudāharaṇam ।</p>
<p>athāśīḥ-- <q>yathāśāstrārthasaṃpannām</q> ityādi । yathā --</p>

1 <q>bha</q>--anekaprakṛtisthitam 2 <q>bha</q>--vacanairyuktaṃ 3 <q>ca</q>--bhāsanaṃ tadbhavet <q>pa</q>--jñeyaṃ nirbhāsanaṃ tu tat 4 <q>ca</q>--anekatvāt
5 <q>pa</q>--yadā 6 <q>bha</q>--śāstre'rthasaṃpattiḥ 7 <q>pa</q>--saṃpannaṃ 8 <q>pa</q>--samudbhavam bha--samudbhavā ।
*bhamātṛkāyāṃ saṃśayasya lakṣaṇaṃ bhidyate
parapraśaṃsāvacanaṃ prayuktaṃ yo'bhyasūyate ।
pūrvottarārthavyāghātaḥ saṃśayaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ ।। iti ।
*pūrṇaḥ śloka :--
rājā duśśāsanādergururanujaśatasyāṅgarājasya mitram ।
kṛṣṇākeśottarīyavyapayanapaṭuḥ pāṇḍavā yasya dāsāḥ
kvāste duryodhano'sau kathayata na ruṣā draṣṭumabhyāgatau svaḥ ।। (veṇīsaṃhārāt)

<lg><l>aprārthanīyāmanyāṃ1 vā vidustāmāśiṣaṃ budhāḥ ।। 28</l></lg>
<lg><l>ādau yatkrodhajananamante harṣapravardhanam ।</l>

<p>"pādāgrasthitayā" (ratnā--1--1)ityādi । sarvaṃ vacanaṃ na cāśīralaṅkāraḥ stutyā eva

prasiddhānāṃ devatādīnāṃ parāpekṣā sādhyākāṃkṣā tasmād vyudāsastatsaṃpattyā ।
ata eva dṛṣṭāntādasya bhedaḥ iti ।</p>
<p>atha priyaṃ --<q>ādau</q> <q>yatkrodhajana</q>namiti । yathā--
<lg><l>kiṃ vṛttāntaiḥ paragṛhagataiḥ kiṃ tu nāhaṃ samarthaḥ</l>

atra bhramati vallabhetyādau krodhajananaṃ hanta kīrtiriti harṣakṛt । anye paṭhanti--
<lg><l>vācyamarthaṃ parityajya dṛṣṭyādibhiranekadhā ।</l>

dṛṣṭirdarśanaṃ prakṛtimukharādivākyamiti pūrvoktamityarthaḥ । na ceyaṃ vyājastutiḥ nindābhāge stuterabhāvāt,
pūrṇatāyāstu nindāyā abhāvāt । yathā vā--</p>
<p>† "pradyotasya sutā" ityuktvā vasantakaṃ vipratārayituṃ rājā

sukhamutpadyate'tīva sā prītiriti kīrtitā ।। iti ।
etaccatuḥṣaṣṭyaṅgamadhye niveśanīyaṃ, na tu lakṣaṇarūpeṇa vyāpāravaicitrīmāpādayati ।

<lg><l>1yatrāpasārayandoṣaṃ guṇamarthena yojayet ।</l>
<l>2guṇābhivādaṃ doṣādvā kāryaṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ viduḥ3 ।। 37</l></lg>
<lg><l>4apūrvakrodhajanitamaparādhaṃ pramṛjya yat5 ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 319 !-->

<p>atha kāryaṃ--<q>yatrāpasārayan doṣa</q>miti । doṣamapasārya guṇaṃ yadātve'rthanīye niyojayati
guṇābhivādaṃ vāpasārya doṣānarthe yojayati āśritya tenārthaṃ yojayatītyarthaḥ । prathama udāharaṇaṃ--</p>
<p>"tāvatsvātmani saṃśritadrumalatāśleṣo'dhvagairvarjanam" ।* ityādi । dvitīye mamaiva--
<lg><l>viśvaprabho vitaratāṃ kamalāṃ kimanyad</l>
<l>bhūyātsa ko'pi ghaṭito bhavatopakāraḥ ।</l>

etatkaiścidgahanamityuktam । anye tvadhīyate--
<lg><l>arthāntarasya kathane yatrānyo'rthaḥ pratīyate ।</l>
<l>vākyamādhuryasaṃpannā sārthāpattiriti smṛtā ।। iti ।</l></lg>
atra hi mahāṃstvayāsyopakāraḥ kṛtaḥ, adhvagānāṃ ca mahadambu dattamityukte, viśvaprabho iti punariti
paryālocanādarthāntarasyāpattiḥ ।</p>
<p>athānunītiḥ -- <q>apūrvakrodhajanitamiti</q> । apūrvasya sātiśayasya krodhasya jananāya
yo'parādhastam । yathā--</p>

<p>atha paridevanaṃ--<q>doṣairyadanyanāmoktai</q>riti । yathā <q>bālarāmāyaṇe</q> daśarathanāmnā ye doṣā uktā

na tu daśarathe tatparidevitaṃ "narendravṛddhaḥ strīvaśaṃ nyastamayasa ।" ityādinā । arthena prayojanena
ye'nyanāmoktā arthāḥ prasiddhārthairyatprayojitaṃ saṃvāditamanyahṛdaye doṣāḥ saṃbandhaṃ saṃbandhanaṃ taccārthena

<l>rmandaṃ mandamakāri yena nijayordordaṇḍayormaṇḍanam ।।</l></lg>

janitaḥ "kiṃ tulyamānuṣatve'rjunaparākramanyūnatā mama tatkiṃ maṇḍanayā adhikārasthānāṃ hyada" iti
tatra paramaucityakhyāpanaṃ prayojanam । unye paṭhanti--

parivartamānatvātpṛthaksiddhenaiva prakṛtavarṇanīyavanitāvadanādi sundarīkriyata iti tadevālaṅkāraḥ ।

saṃnidhirupamānopameyadyotakasādhāraṇadharmāṇāṃ kvacidantarlīnenopamānopameyamekīkriyate tatra
rūpakavyavahāraḥ । tatra hi padārthe prayujyamānaḥ śabda ivārthaṃ garbhīkarotīti nyāyaḥ । kvacittu
ekapraghaṭṭakāvasthānabalādupamāgatiḥ, yathā dīpake । upalakṣaṇaṃ caitadvaicitryāntarāṇām ।।</p>
<p><q>upādhyāyamataṃ</q> tu --lakṣaṇabalādalaṅkārāṇāṃ vaicitryamāgacchati tathā hi--guṇānuvādanāmnā

vyākurvate ca--rūpakaśabdasyānvarthākhyāyakametat, aupamyasya guṇatvena pradhānatayā saṃśrayo yatra
tathā kṛtvā rūpasya yānyarūpeṇa niścitya varṇanā tadrūpakam । kathaṃ tanniścaya ityāha nānābhūtena
pṛtagbhūtenāpi dravyeṇa yo'nurāgaḥ sphaṭikasyeva lākṣayā tata ādigrahaṇād
bhrāntigauṇalākṣaṇikādibhedānāṃ grahaṇam (iti) ।</p>
<p>evamarthaviṣayalakṣaṇaprasaṅgenārthālaṅkārān pradarśya śabdālaṅkārasvarūpamāha <q>śabdābhyāsastu</q>

tenaikasyākṣarasya padasya vā dvitīyaṃ sadṛśaṃ nirantaraṃ sāntaraṃ vā śobhājanakamalaṅkāraḥ । yathā
muktāphalasyocitamuktāphalāntarapadmarāgādervopāśrayaviśeṣaḥ samucitasahāsīna--
satpuruṣa--madhyapatanaṃ vā satpuruṣāntarasya । pāde <q>ādi</q>grahaṇaṃ tadā madhyāntādiṣu
vikalpitavacanānnāstyapi sthāpananiyamo'nuprāsalāṭīyādisaṃgrahāyetyāha । <q>viśeṣadarśana</q>miti

<p>arthahīnaṃ yathā--"adyāpi smarasi ( ?smarati) rasālasaṃ mano me mugdhāyāḥ smaracaturāṇi"।
(vāmana 2.2.10, udāharaṇa) atrapūrvāparavyāghātādasaṃbandhatā । yathā vā " sa mahātmā
bhāgyavaśānmahāpatha( ?da) mupāgataḥ" । (vāmana 2, 2, 20, udāharaṇa) iti । atra hi sāvaśeṣaḥ

<p>grāmyaṃ yathā--"bhadre bhajasva māmidaṃ te dāsyāmi " iti । tṛtīyaṃ bhinnārthaṃ yathā--"syāccedeṣa
na rāvaṇaḥ" ityuktvā, "kva nu punaḥ sarvatra sarveguṇāḥ" iti । uddiṣṭaṃ hyatra rāvaṇasyānupādeyatvaṃ
kva nu punarityenanānyathākaraṇādbheditam । *</p>
<p>ekārthaṃ yathā--"kundenduhāraharahāsasitaṃ" iti । ekaprayojanaṃ hi sarvametat । na hi kāvyaṃ
śāstravadupadeśyaṃ kaścitkiṃcijjānīyāditi pravartate ।</p>

<lg><l>su(sau)vīreṣvasti nagarī mathurā nāma viśrutā ।</l>
<l>akṣoṭanālikerāḍhyā yasyāḥ paryantabhūmayaḥ । ityādi । †</l></lg>
<p>viṣamaṃ yathā--"ayi paśyasi saudhamāśritāmavirasumanomālabhāriṇīm "(vāmana 2.2.2)
ityādi । yadi ( ?visandhi) doṣo'nenaiva saṃgṛhītaḥ sandhānaṃ dvayornairantaryaṃ vicārayogaḥ
anyonyalayo veti tridhā tadanupārūḍhamayuktaṃ pāruṣyādyutpādakaṃ vā yatrāpaśabdaḥ smṛto
<q>munitrayeṇādṛtaḥ</q> । etanmadhye tu kecit ' nityadoṣāḥ, yathā apaśabdaḥ, kecidanityā yathā--grāmyaṃ
hāsyādau tasyeṣṭatamatvāt । etadāha yathāsthūlamiti । ānupūrvyaṃ, [iti cātra]1 avyayenāvyayībhāvaḥ
tenottarottaraṃ [sthūlāḥ]2 । ete doṣāḥ sthūlāḥ yathā ca gūḍhārthaṃ gūḍhalekhaprahelikā(di) patākāsthānakādiṣu
prayojyam, arthāntaramanuvāde, arthahīnādi hāsye, bhinnārthaṃ śrotriyādau vaktari, ekārthaṃ parapratyāyane,
abhiplutārthamunmādādau, bhinnavṛttaṃ ca visandhi [ca] svaviṣaye । evamete doṣāḥ krameṇāpātaviṣayāḥ।
iha yato'rthapratītistāvadasti apaśabdastu doṣa eva tataḥ kasyāścidarthapratīterabhāvāt sa hi na
kāṃcidbhāṣāmanupatati saṅketābhāvāttamarthaṃ pratipādayet ।</p>

<lg><l>śleṣaḥ prasādaḥ samatā samādhi--</l>

<l>kāntiśca kāvyasya guṇā daśaite* ।। 96</l></lg>
<lg><l>1īpsitenārthajātena saṃbaddhānāṃ parasparam ।</l>

<p>anye'pi guṇāḥ santīti darśayati śleṣaḥ prasāda ityādi । <q>kāvyasye</q>ti padasya vākyasya

<lg><l>dṛṣṭvaikāsanasaṃsthite (saṅgate) priyatame paścādupetyādarā--</l>

yenāsaṃbhāvanāspadaṃ na bhavati tena kuṭilo'pyayaṃ kramo na hṛdaye ulbaṇatvaṃ bhajate majjati hṛdaye
yataḥ sarvasyeti ।</p>

prasādamādhuryasaukumāryakāntilakṣaṇānāmeva pāṭhe saṃvāditvaṃ dṛśyate । pāṭhadvaividhyaṃ kvacit traividhyaṃ ca vidyate ।

<p>atha śabdaguṇamāha nityārthe padānāṃ śliṣṭatā parasparaṃ yoniḥ sandhibandhanatayānekamekapadamiva
bhāti tadeva māsṛṇyamucyate । ataśca padāntarapāṭhasyāvaśyāpekṣatāyāṃ yathā brahmāsūtramiti । uktaṃ
caitacchando'dhyāye । tathā sandhīyamānayostathāsandheḥ sājātyaṃ sāvarṇyaṃ ca saṃpadyate vastrakhaṇḍayoriva
sūtrasyeva ca । yathā--"astyuttarasyāṃ diśi devatātmā" (kumā 1--1)(vāmana 3.2.6 udāharaṇa)
asti śabdasyottaraśabdasya sandhīyamānayostakāreṇa takāreṇa saṃyoge tayośca sājātyaṃ, 'syāndiśi'
ityanayoḥ sandhernakārasya vargyatvāddakāreṇa sāvarṇyaṃ, 'diśi devatā' iti nairantarya ( ?sāntarya) sandhau
dakāreṇa sājātyaṃ, ikāraikārayostālavyāṃśatvena sādṛśyaṃ, 'devatātmā' ityatra takāremākāreṇa
ca । na cānuprāsamātrametat, ekapadānuprāse'pi prāmāṇyabhāvāt --'indindirāṇāṃ lalito ninādaḥ'
ityanuprāse ca sāvarṇyenopayogīti । anye paṭhanti --vicāragahanaṃ yatsyāt sphuṭaṃ caiva svabhāvataḥ
। ityarthaśleṣaḥ vakraghaṭamānaṃ ( ? vakraghaṭanā)1 vetyarthaḥ suparatibaddhaśca śleṣa iti padaśleṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>prasādamāha--<q>apyanukto</q> budhairiti । yatrārthe anukte'pi budhaiḥ kaṣṭakalpanayā
avyākhyato'pyarthaḥ prayojanaṃ svayaṃ jāyate so'rtho vaimalyāśrayo'pi vaimalyamupacārāt
so'rtho vā kāvyasya vaimalyaṃ svayaṃ jānaṃścānupayogiparivarjanāt । vaimalyaśabdavācyājjalasyeva
pāṃsubhirasaṃparkādbhavatīti vaimalyamarthasya prasādaḥ । yathā --"savarṇā kanyakā rūpayauvanārambhaśālinī"
iti vivāhyatvaṃ prāpaṇīyatāhṛdyatvaṃ saṃbhogayogyatā, gṛhasthasahadharmacāriṇītvamityupayogī
sarvo'yamarthaḥ । tenābudhvaitadudāharaṇāntaraṃ vṛthā bhramaṇam--"āvilapayodharāgra" miti (vikramo
5--8) etadapi tūdāharaṇaṃ padadūṣaṇaṃ tu samyagajñāne prayuktam ( ?)। aprasādastu

<lg><l>bhūṣaṇākṣarasaṅghātau śobhodāharaṇe tathā ।</l>
<l>hetusaṃśayadṛṣṭāntāḥ prāptyabhiprāya eva ca ।। 1</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 348 !-->
<p>†samastārthālaṅkāravargasya bījabhūtāścamatkārāḥ kathāśarīravaicitryadāyino vakroktirūpā
lakṣaṇaśabdena vyavahriyante । lakṣaṇāni guṇālaṅkāramahimānamanapekṣya svasaubhāgyenaiva śobhante ।
lakṣaṇaṃ mahāpuruṣasya padmādirekhādivatkāvyaśarīrasya saundaryadāyi । alaṅkārastu ratnābharaṇādivadeva,
yena vināpi svasaundaryeṇaiva puruṣaḥ, pravibhāsate । guṇastu pravṛttidyotito dhairyādivatkāvyasya
śabdārtharacanāmāśrayati । yathā lakṣaṇarahitaḥ puruṣo na sundaraśabdavācyastathālakṣaṇavarjaṃ kathāśarīraṃ
guṇālaṅkārojjvalamapi nīrasatvaṃ bhajatprauḍhakāvyābhidhānaṃ nārhati । kathāśarīrasaṃpanneṣu kāvyeṣveva
lakṣaṇāni nirvartyante na tu muktakādiṣu khaṇḍakāvyeṣu, ata eva 'kāvyabandhāstu kartavyā' (nā.śā.
15/227) iti muninaiva muktakādivāraṇaparamuktam । lakṣaṇānyasaṃkhyeyāni, teṣāṃ
camatkṛtiviśeṣagariṣṭhāṇi ṣaṭtriṃśadeva <q>muninā</q> saṃgṛhītāni । <q>kohalā</q>dibhistacchiṣyaiḥ
prakīrtitānyaparāṇi kānicillakṣaṇatvena prasiddhimupagatāni kālapravāhe bharatagrantha eva
pāṭhāntaranibandharūpeṇa prakṣiptāni syuḥ । saundaryajanakatvakāraṇena <q>bhojā</q>dibhirubhayapāṭhagatānyapi
lakṣaṇāni svīkṛtyānyairapi kaiściccamatkṛtibhūtairlakṣaṇaiḥ saha catuḥṣaṣṭitvena prakaṭitāni ।</p>
<p>yadvivecitamatigambhīraprauḍhavācā <q>bhagavatā vṛttikāreṇa</q> lakṣaṇānyasaṃkhyānīti tadupaṣṭabhyaiva
bhinnapāṭho'pi bālānāṃ samupavedya ityabhūhya tanmadhya eva saṃkṣepeṇa prakāśitaḥ ।</p>
<p>bhūṣaṇaṃ lakṣayati-- alaṅkārairiti <q>bharato</q>ktairupamādibhirguṇaiśca yatra kathā--
śarīraracanā samullāsitā tadbhūṣaṇaṃ nāma lakṣaṇam । citrārthairiti vibhāvādi--

(bhaṭṭanāyaka, hṛdayadarpaṇe) "dve vartmanī giro devyāḥ śāstraṃ ca kavikarma ca । prajñopajñantayorādyaṃ
pratibhodbhavamantimam" (bhaṭṭatotasya) ityādinā bhojakuntalakabhaṭṭanāyakatotādibhiruktarītyā
guṇālaṅkāravargaḥ sarva eva lakṣaṇaśabdena parigṛhītaḥ । guṇālaṅkāraireva yatra kathārūpā vakroktiratiśayitā

yathā vā kathāśarīrasaṃghaṭanavaicitryarūpaśobhāyā abhijñānaśakuntalāyāṃ madhuraraprasaktiḥ ।</p>
<p>pareṣāṃ durbhedyaparamārthena tulyārthaprayuktena vākyena nigūḍhāśaya kasmaicinnipuṇairyatra

āṇaṃ'' ityupadiśati । atrābhisaraṇameva pradyumnasaṅgamopāya ityarthaḥ sādhyate ।</p>
<p>hetuḥ--phalasādhanaśaktiyuktaṃ mitaśabdārthaṃ vicitrabhaṅgyuktaṃ vacanam । yathā
tāpasavatsarāje ṣaṣṭhe'ṅke kṛtamaraṇaniścayāṃ vāsavadattāṃ paribodhayanyaugandharāyaṇa āha--devi prasīda,
<lg><l>āsṛṣṭeḥ pratipārthivaṃ yuvatayo jātā manovallabhāḥ</l>

(tāpasavatsarāje ṣaṣṭhe'ṅke)
devyā yat kṛtaṃ tadiṣṭārthasādhanameva acireṇaiva śubhaphalamanubhavasīti ।</p>

<lg><l>1abhipretārthasiddhayarthaṃ kīrtyante yatra sūribhiḥ ।</l>
<l>prayojanānyanekāni sā māletyabhisaṃjñitā ।। 29</l></lg>
<lg><l>hṛṣṭaiḥ prasannavadanairyatparasyānuvartanam2 ।</l>
<l>kriyate vākyaceṣṭābhistaddākṣiṇyamudāhṛtam3 ।। 30</l></lg>
<lg><l>yatra saṃkīrtayandoṣaṃ4 guṇamarthena darśayet ।</l>
<l>5guṇātipātāddoṣānvā 6garhaṇaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।। 31</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 359 !-->
iti khaṅgamākarṣati । tadā prahastaḥ (ubhayormadhye nipatya)--prasīdatu prasīdatu, mahārājaḥ, nedamanurūpaṃ
svāminaḥ । deva--
<lg><l>lokatrayakṣayodvṛttaprakopāgresarasya te ।</l>
<l>īdṛśaścandrahāsasya bhṛtyeṣvanucitaḥ kramaḥ ।। iti । (rāmābhyudaye dvitīye'ṅke)</l></lg>
mālā yathā rājā--
<lg><l>dṛṣṭā yūyaṃ nirjitā vidviṣantaḥ prāptā devī bhūtadhātrī ca bhūyaḥ ।</l>
<l>saṃbandho'bhūddarśakenāpi sārdhaṃ kiṃ duṣprāpaṃ yanna labdhaṃ bhavadbhayaḥ ।। iti tāpasavatsarāje</l></lg>
dākṣiṇyaṃ yathā ratnāvalyāṃ dvitīye'ṅke śīrṣavedanavyājena gantumudyatāṃ vāsavadattāṃ paṭāntena gṛhītvā
nirundhan vatsarājaḥ "priye, prasīdeti brūyām" (ratnāvalī 2/19)ityādi vadanniṣkrāntāyāṃ preyasyāṃ
"alamaraṇyaruditena" iti bruvantaṃ vidūṣakamāha--"mūḍha ! na lakṣitastvayā devyāḥ kopaḥ tatsarvathā
devīprasādanaṃ muktvā nānyamatropāyamākalayāmi । tadehi devīṃ prasādayitumabhyantarameva praviśāvaḥ"
iti । atra rājño'nuvartanaṃ dākṣiṇyam ।
garhaṇaṃ deṣasya guṇīkṛtatvaṃ * yathā--
<lg><l>praṇaṣṭā na vyaktirbhavati vacasaḥ saiva mṛdutā</l>
<l>na rāgo netrābje tyajati na ca lajjā vyapagatā ।</l>
<l>smṛtiḥ pratyāyātā parihṛṣitamadyāpi ca mukhaṃ</l>
<l>mado doṣāṃstyaktvā tvayi pariṇatastiṣṭhati guṇaiḥ ।। (dhūrtaviṭe)</l></lg>

<lg><l>1arthāntarasya kathane yatrānyo'rthaḥ 2apratīyate2 ।</l>

<lg><l>vākyaiḥ sātiśayairuktā vākyārthasya prasādhakaiḥ4 ।</l>

<l>sācivyato nāparamasti puṃsāṃ viṣādaduḥkhāyaśasāṃ nidānam ।।</l></lg>
(vatsarājacarite dvitīye'ṅke)
yathā vā lāmakāyanaḥ--
<lg><l>pūrvāhṇe kṛtabhojanavyatikarānnityaiva nīrogatā</l>
<l>kaṇḍūtirvapanādapaiti śirasaḥ snānaṃ yadā rocate ।</l>

<l>dhūrtaiḥ sattvahitāya kairapi kṛtaṃ sādhuvrataṃ saugatam ।। (tāpasavatsarāje tṛtīya'ṅke)</l></lg>
arthāpattiryathā --
<lg><l>ādaṣṭasphuritādhare bhavati yo vaktrāravinde rasaḥ</l>
<l>prītiryā ca hṛtāṃśuke ca jaghane kāñjīprabhoddayotite ।</l>
<l>lakṣmīryā ca nakhakṣatāṅkuradhare pīne kapole striyo</l>
<l>raktaṃ tena virajyate na hṛdayaṃ jātyantare'pi dhruvam ।। (dhūrtaviṭe)</l></lg>
atra janmāntare'pi tasyā anuraktiranurvartata evetyukte janmāntareṣvapi virāgo na prabhavati
tasmādbhavabandhavimuktirna syādityarthāpattirnāma lakṣaṇam ।</p>
<p>prasiddhiḥ --prasādhakaiḥ prakṛṣṭasādhakaiḥ, prasiddhaiḥ pūrvameva siddhaiḥ । yathā baladevaḥ
duryodhanamāha--bhīmasena idānīṃ tava yuddhavañcanāmutpādya sthāsyati ।</p>
<lg><l>duryo--kiṃ cāhaṃ bhīmasenena vañcitaḥ ।</l>

<lg><l>yatrākārodbhavairvākyairātmānamathavā param ।</l>
<l>1pṛcchannivābhidhatte'rthaṃ sā pṛcchetyabhisaṃjñitā ।। 34</l></lg>
<lg><l>dṛṣṭa2śrutānubhūtārtha 3kathanādi samudbhavam ।</l>

<p>duryo- śrūyatāṃ,
<lg><l>yenendrasya ca pārijātakatarurmānena tulyaṃ hṛto</l>

<l>dīptyā bhīmagadāṃ praviśya sahasā nirvyājayuddhapriyaḥ</l>
<l>tenāhaṃ jagatāṃ priyeṇa hariṇā mṛtyoḥ pratigrāhitaḥ ।। (gadāyuddhe)*</l></lg>
atra vākyārthasya sādhakā eva bhagavato viṣṇoḥ pārijātāharaṇalīlāvaṭapatraśayanādayaḥ । anye
tu prasādakairalaṅkāribhiriti gṛhṇanti ।</p>
<p>pṛcchā śokādiparavaśatayātmānaṃ vā paraṃ vā parokṣe saṃbodhya pṛcchannivābhidhānam ।

yathā hanumān sītāṃ dṛṣṭāha--
<lg><l>sthāne'vasīdasi raghūdvaha kiṃ vidhātaḥ</l>
<l>asyāstvayekṣitamalakṣaṇamaṅgakeṣu ।</l>
<l>adyāpi jīvasi daśānana he hanūman</l>
<l>keyaṃ tavābhimukhavarti ripoḥ pratīkṣā।। iti । (rāmacarite)</l></lg>
<p>sārūpyaṃ--ādiśabdena darśanaśravaṇānubhavanānyupalakṣitāni । atra rūpavibhrāntyā na
kṣobhajananameva lakṣaṇasya camatkṛtiḥ । yathā chalitarāme lakṣmaṇena badhvānīto lavo
rāmayajñaśālāyāṃ hiraṇmayīṃ sītāṃ dṛṣṭvāha--"aye kathamiyamambā rājadvāramāgatā" iti sahasotthāya
praṇamya tadanantaraṃ kāñcanamayīti nirvarṇyopasṛtyopaviśati ।।</p>
<p>yathā vā --duryodhanaṃ hatvāgacchantaṃ bhīmasenaṃ duryodhanamiti cārvākavārtayaiva bhrāntvā dharmasūnustaṃ
gāḍhaṃ gṛhītvāha....</p>

<lg><l>hṛdayasthasya vākyasya 1agūḍhārthasya vibhāvakam1 ।</l>

<lg><l>yadvākyaṃ 3vākyakuśalairupāyonābhidhīyate ।</l>

<l>mugdhānanāmarajasaṃ kalikāmakāle

<l>atrātmānameva sumanolatātvenāpadiśati ।।</l></lg>
<p>leśo yathā <q>vimārake dvitīye'ṅke</q> dhātrī nāyakamāha--ayya kiṃ ciṃtīadi
avimārakaḥ -- bhavati śāstraṃ cintyate ।
<lg><l>dhātrī --kiṃ ṇāma edaṃ ramaṇijjaṃ satthaṃ ciṃtīadi ।</l></lg>
<lg><l>avi--bhavati yogaśāstraṃ cintyate ।</l></lg>
<lg><l>dhātrī--(sasmitaṃ) paḍiggahīdaṃ maṃgalavaaṇaṃ, joasatthaṃ evva hodu ।</l></lg>
avi-ko nu khalu vākyārthaḥ । anyadapyabhilāṣavaśādanyathā saṃkalpayāmi । ityādi ।
anye tu lekha iti paṭhanniṅgitajñānābhidhānamiti ca lakṣayanti ।</p>
<p>kṣobho yathā <q>ratnāvalyāṃ</q> tṛtīye'ṅke sāgarikaiveti matvā vāsavadattāmupalālayato rājñaḥ
sā svāvaguṇṭhanamapanīya vailakṣyamutpāditavatī ।</p>

piavaassassa ।</p>
<p>vāsa--ṇaṃ puḍhamasaṃgame vigdhaṃ karaṃtīe mae jevva edassa avaraddhaṃ ṇa ajjaputtassa।</p>

<p>guṇakīrtanaṃ yathā <q>vatsarājacarite</q> cutarthe'ṅke śālaṅkāyanaḥ--nīlanāgavyapadeśena samantataḥ

<p>tena proktaṃ dhairyagāmbhīryaśauryaprajñātejonītidākṣiṇyagarbham ।</p>
<p>vākyaṃ sāmādyaṃ sorjitaṃ śrotraramyaṃ śāstrīkartavyaṃ tadbudhaiḥ svārthakāmaiḥ।। (vatsarājacarite)
bharatarohakaḥ --eṣa saṃkṣiptavistaro nāma ।</p>

<p><q>śrīḥ</q></p>
<p><q>nāṭyaśāstram</q></p>
<p>saptadaśo'dhyāyaḥ*</p>
<lg><l>1evaṃ tu saṃskṛtaṃ pāṭhyaṃ mayā proktaṃ samāsataḥ2 ।</l>
<l>3prākṛtasya tu pāṭhyasya saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। 1</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 365 !-->
<lg><l>yadāntararasāsvādakākuviśrāntisundaram ।</l>
<l>rasākṣapakṣagaṃ vande tadvapuḥ pārameśvaram ।। (abhinavaguptasya)</l></lg>
<p>caturdaśādhyāye vācikoktakrame saṃskṛtaṃ prākṛtaṃ ca vākyamityuktam । tatra saṃskṛtaprasaṅgena
chandovṛttalakṣaṇādi nirūpitam । anena tvadhyāyena prākṛtasya svarūpaṃ nirupyate ।
śāstraprasiddhasaṃskṛtaviparītaprākṛtaprasaṅgena nāmadheyibhāgarūparūpaṇaṃ śāstravihitānāṃ
viparītarūpatvāt, nāṭyasamayapātino bhāvamāriṣādināmasamūhasya paṭhanadharmāśca prākṛte'pi kimanyathā
saṃskṛtavadveti cintāyāṃ prasaṅgena kāryasvarūpaṃ nirūpitam । daśarūpakanirṇayānantaraṃ samucitanirṇayamapi
tatā--
<lg><l>alaṅkārā virāmāśca ye pāṭhye saṃskṛte matāḥ ।</l>
<l>ta eva yatnataḥ kāryāḥ strīpāṭhye'pi ca saṃskṛte ।। (17-133)</l></lg>
ityadhyāyopānte prākṛtapāṭhyamevopasaṃhariṣyāmītyadhyāyasaṅgatiḥ । etāmeva
darśayati <q>evaṃ tu saṃskṛta</q>mityādi । pāṭhaviśeṣamarhati, yatnena vā paṭhanīyaṃ, viśiṣṭena
<!-- APPARATUS page 365 !-->
1 <q>dara</q>--etattu <q>bha</q>-- pāṭhyaṃ tu saṃskṛtaṃ viprāḥ 2 <q>ḍa</q>-- dvijottamāḥ 3 <q>ja</q>--prākṛtasyāpi
* <q>jādibā</q>nteṣu rasaṃjñake N saṃjñake cāṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ । asminnadhyāye prākṛtalakṣaṇapāṭhaḥ sarveṣvādarśeṣu
sarvābaddhamayaḥ । <q>naya</q>yoreva teṣāṃ sādhiṣṭha iti vṛttikāreṇa dattānāṃ pratīkānāṃ ca saṃvādabahulatvācca tayoḥ pāṭha eva
mūlarupeṇa niveśitaḥ । prākṛtalakṣaṇaślokānāṃ vyākhyānasāpekṣatvādagre'nubandharūpeṇa saṃkṣepeṇa ṭīkā yojyate ।

<lg><l>etadeva viparyastaṃ saṃskāraguṇavarjitam ।</l>
<l>vijñeyaṃ prākṛtaṃ pāṭhyaṃ nānāvasthāntarātmakam ।। 2</l></lg>
<lg><l>trividhaṃ tacca1 vijñeyaṃ nāṭyayoge2 samāsataḥ ।</l>
<l>samānaśabdaṃ vibhraṣṭaṃ3 deśīgatamathāpi ca4 ।। 3</l></lg>
<lg><l>(5pāṭhyamekaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ prākṛtaṃ yathā6 ।)</l>
<l>7kamalāmalareṇutaraṅgalola8salilādivākyasaṃpannam ।</l>
<l>prākṛtabandheṣvevaṃ9 10saṃskṛtamapi yogamupayāti ।। 4</l></lg>
