rūpeṇa vā paṭhanārhaṃ āntaracittavṛttivaśādeva vā tathā paṭhituṃ śakyaṃ,
ācāryayatnena vā paṭhanīyamiti pāṭhyam । tatra prākṛtasya sāmānyalakṣaṇamāha (saṃskāreti)saṃskṛtameva
saṃskāraguṇena yatnena parirakṣārūpeṇa varjitaṃ prākṛtaṃ, prakṛterasaṃskārarūpāyā āgatam ।</p>
<p>nanvapabhraṃśānāṃ ko niyama ityāha <q>nānā</q> yānyavasthāntarāṇi deśaviśeṣāsteṣvātmā
niyatasvabhāvo yasyāṃ, deśaviśeṣeṣu prasiddhyā niyamitamityeva saṃskṛtā eva vācakāḥ anumānāttvanye
te tvanyatve prasiddhiṃ gatā ityuktam । avatiṣṭhante'nyasminnityavasthāḥ deśāḥ । saṃskṛte same'pi
prātipadike vibhaktau bhavitavyaṃ viparyāsena svareṇa vā deśīpadamapi svarasyaiva prayogāvasare
prayujyata iti tadapi prākṛtameva, avyutpāditaprakṛ testajjanaprayojyatvāt prākṛtamiti kecit ।
saṃskṛtena samānaśabdānudāharati <q>kamalāma</q>leti । vibhaktau liṅgasya prākṛte svātantryādavaśyaṃ bhedena
bhāvyamityāha vākye samāsopapannaṃ yojitam । etatparijñānasya phalamāha <q>evaṃ saṃskṛtamapi</q>
<q>yoga</q>miti । bhāṣāśleṣe patākāsthānakādau cāsya prayoga uktaḥ । <q>api</q> śabdenedamāha prākṛtaprayoge
samāse'pi na saṃskṛtasamateti kamala amala indu ityādau ।</p>

7 <q>bha</q>--kamaladalareṇukesarataraṅgasalilādi 8 <q>da</q>--jālādi <q>na</q> --salīlādi <q>ṭa</q>--jhaḍitphasaṃpadam( ?) 9 <q>bha</q>--etat

<lg><l>śārīryāmatha vīṇāyāṃ tribhyaḥ sthānebhya eva tu1 ।</l>

kāye niṣpadyamānā tāratvaṃ saṃpādayantī evaṃ tāramandramadhyatā savarṇānāṃ sarvaṃ (svara ?)

ṣaṭṣaṣṭisthānabhedanivṛttyartham । tathā hyuraḥsthāne dvāviśaṃti sthānāni yatra śrutayaḥ svarāśca । evaṃ

śobhāsaṃpādanadūraśravaṇādiprayojanā svarakākuḥ sā tena vakṣyata iti । evaṃ praṣṭavyāstāvat--
yo'yaṃ svarakākorviṣaya uktastatra yadyartharūpaṃ kiṃcidabhidheyaṃ tatrāvaśyamarthakākorvā
pṛthaksvarakākuḥ । tathā hi nepathyapāṭhe'pi kañcukī paṭhati 'vīro'yamaṅgadaḥ paṭhati,
'yaugandharāyaṇaḥ paṭhati' iti, evaṃ bhūtavṛttacittavṛttyādiviśeṣapratipādakenaiva pāṭhena bhavitavyam ।
vaitālīyapāṭhe'pi samucitāvasarāvedanapradhāne'vaśyamartha ādātavya eva । uktaṃ caitat--
arthānapekṣayā kimabhinayanamanyacintayā, pustakavācakapāṭho hyanukriyamāṇo'bhinayatāmavalambate ।
anyathābhinayarūpatvābhāve tadupakaraṇadharmyāditatphalarasādivyatiriktatve
svarātodyagānādivailakṣaṇye ca cintayaiva kiṃ prayojanamiti । na syātkākusāmānyalakṣaṇametena kiṃ
ghaṭata ityanye । eva<q>mapi bhavatī</q>tyasamarthitaṃ syāt taddhi pūrvaprakāntavastusamarthanena prayujyata iti muneḥ
śaulī । tasmātpūrvoktasthānatrayasamarthanārtho'yaṃ ślokaḥ । tadayamarthaḥ-- śārīryāṃ vīṇāyāṃ

<lg><l>1ābhāṣaṇaṃ ca dūrasthe śirasā saṃprayojayet ।</l>

kāśadeśaparigrahārthaṃ, na śarīramātre svaraniṣpattiḥ, api tu tatraiva । yeyaṃ bāhyavīṇādaṇḍasthānīyā
uttarottarasthānaparamparāviśiṣṭā, sā sthānasopānapaṅktiḥ svaraniṣpattisthānam, ata eva kākusvaramapi
lakṣitam--kaka laulye,* laulyaṃ ca sākāṃkṣate yathā (?sākāṃkṣatā iyatā. Raghavan)
svaravaicitryaṃ lakṣyate īṣadyato vācyabhūmiḥ saṃpadyate sā kākuḥ, īṣadarthe kuśabdasya kādeśaḥ।
kākurvā jihvā tadvyāpārasaṃpādyatvāt kākuḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ sthānasvarūpaṃ vibhajya tasya viṣayabhedamādarśayitumāhaḥ <q>ābhāṣaṇaṃ ca dūrastha</q> ityādi ।
śiraseti śironiṣpannena nodanetyarthaḥ । nātidūre kaṇṭheneti madhyena, urasā samīpe mandreṇeti yāvat ।</p>

ślokārthaḥ । yadā hi na dīptena krodhādinā nāpi mandrarūpeṇa śokādināviṣṭahṛdayo bhavati tadā
krameṇa vaktavyavastuviṣayotsāhavisphāraṇāt tārāntaṃ gacchannupasaṃhāre madhya eva viśrāmyatītya--
navaśiṣṭasyāyaṃ (?tyaviśiṣṭasyā) sāmānyena pāṭhadharmaḥ । ata eva śānte

na tadviṣaye svarakākuḥ । kastarhi tasyā viṣayaḥ, ucyate--kadācidarthasya dharmapuñjavācyasya

<!-- COMMENTARY page 400 !-->
yadi svalpākṣarāṇi padānyasamastāni bhavanti । bahvakṣarapade, daridrāśca kiṃ yaste (?) ityādau
na madhye sūcāṅkurayorupapattiḥ ।</p>
<p>"tasyāstanumukhamasti saumyasubhagaṃ kiṃ pārvaṇenendunā"* (vāmana 4/3/27
upamānākṣepa--udāharaṇam) ityādau tu tasyā ityuktvā madhye sūcayā tadityasādhāraṇaviśeṣasmaraṇaṃ
svātmani taccāvalokane tathākarṇane ca pracchannasthitāyā nāyikāyā nivṛttyaṅkure vaicitryaṃ punaḥ
paricumbanābhilāṣasūcāyogapūrvakaṃ mukhamiti pāṭhastatkṛto nāyikāyā raṇaraṇakādaradarśako
nivṛttyaṅkura ityādi vaicitrye utprekṣaṇīyam । aṅkurastvanirvacana eveti nivṛttyaṅkura evātra
mantavyaḥ । yatrāṅkuro bhaviṣyati tadviṣayametaditi tvasat, puṣpāvacayanāṭane yadocitaparikramaṇādau
pūrvabhāvinā svalpākṣareṇa padayogena vaicitryābhāvāt ।</p>
<p>athāsya vicchedasyāṅgasya prādhānyaṃ darśayati--<q>evaṃ virāma</q> ityādi । asminniti virāme
satyabhinayasthito yathāviṣayaṃ prayoktuṃ śakyaḥ । sa ca virāmādgamyate । virāme satyarthaṃ darśayati
abhinaye'nyathā asamañjasatvaṃ syāditi tātparyam । yadi vābhinayo virāme sthita ityabhinayakāryaṃ
virāma evodvahatīti tātparyam । tadāha <q>tatra</q> <q>vyagrā</q>viti । pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭiprādhānyatātparyeṇetya--

1 <q>ḍa</q>-- bhavatyapi ca ślokaḥ 1a: N: bhavatyapi 2 <q>ya</q>--virāme tu prayatnastu 2 a: N: prayatnastu 3 <q>bha</q>--pratiṣṭhitaḥ
<q>na</q> --sthitaḥ <q>ḍa</q>-- hyasmādarthāpekṣī yatastataḥ <q>ca</q>--hyarthe arthāpekṣī yataḥ sthitaḥ 4 <q>da</q>-- samanvitaiḥ 5 <q>da</q>--vāciko'bhinayaḥ
6 <q>ḍa</q>-- darśibhiḥ ।
*saundaryasya padaṃ dṛśau ca yadi te kiṃ nāma nīlotpalaiḥ ।
kiṃ vā komalakāntibhiḥ kisalayaiḥ satyeva tatrādhare
hī dhātuḥ punaruktavasturacanārambheṣvapūrvo grahaḥ ।।﻿<pb n="401"/>

<p>aṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ†</p>
<lg><l>1vartayiṣyāmyahaṃ viprā daśarūpavikalpanam ।</l>
<l>nāmataḥ karmataścaiva tathā caiva prayogataḥ ।। 1</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 406 !-->
<lg><l>rūpaṃ yadetadbahudhā cakāsti tadyena bhāvī bhavitā na jātu ।</l>
<l>taccakṣurarkātmakamīśvarasya vande vapustaijasasāradhāmraḥ ।।</l></lg>
<p>daśarūpopakārikākvādiyojanamiti tatsvarūpaṃ vaktavyamiti saṅgatiruktaiva <q>tadvartayiṣyāmī</q>ti
kimanenocyate, tadasya prayojanaṃ pradarśyate । kaścidevamāśaṅkate, "rasā bhāvā" (a, 6--10)
ityādi sūtrasārasaṅagrahe daśarūpaśabdasya nāmāpi na śrutaṃ, tatkathamuktaṃ daśarūpavidhāne pāṭhyamiti taṃ
pratyāha <q>vartayiṣyā</q>mīti । rūpyate pratyakṣīkriyate yo'rthaḥ tadvācakatvātkāvyāni rūpāṇi1 daśānāṃ
rūpāṇāṃ vibhāgaḥ kalpyate asmāditi <q>daśarūpavikalpanaṃ</q> sūtraṃ tenāyaṃ ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ daśarūpamiti ।
tena bahuvrīhau daśarūpaṃ kāvyamiti bhedāntarāpākaraṇaṃ syādityāśaṃkya dviguḥ, pātrādiprakṣepaśca yo
vyākhyātastatprayāsamātrameva । tadayamarthaḥ --yataḥ sūtrādāṅgiko vācikaśabde prakṛtipratyayārthavibhāgaḥ
kalpyate tatra vāgbhāga evāyaṃ vitatya varṇyate, tena tadeva sūtraṃ varṇitam vivaraṇena prapañcitaṃ bhavatīti
nānirdiṣṭaṃ nirūpyate kiñciditi । <q>nāmata</q> ityuddeśena <q>karma</q>ta iti lakṣaṇena kriyate, tena
<!-- APPARATUS page 406 !-->
†<q>kakhagaghacabhama</q>--mātṛkāsvaṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ । <q>da</q> N--ādarśe ekonaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ । sarveṣvanyeṣu viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।
<q>gaghacamapāyeṣu</q> vyākhyānusārī pāṭho dṛśyate, yasmin lāsyāṅgalakṣaṇamaṣṭādaśe na vartate kiṃtvekonaviṃśa eva dṛśyate ।
bhamātṛkāyāṃ lāsyāṅgalakṣṇāni tālādhyāye (31) varṇitāni । trayodaśa vīthyaṅgānyapi vṛttikāreṇāṣṭādaśe
yānyuktāni bhamātṛkāyāṃ vṛttivikalpe saṃcitāni tāni । ayamaparo viśeṣaḥ --bhamātṛkāyāṃ daśarūpalakṣaṇaṃ
sandhyaṅgalakṣaṇaṃ caikasminnadhyāya eva paṭhitaṃ, yadanyāsu dvayorlakṣitam । tasmāt bhamātṛkāpaṭhita ekonaviṃśaḥ,
abhinavaguptena viṃśa iti, <q>da</q> mātṛkāyāmekaviṃśa iti, tadanyāsu dvāviṃśa iti ca saṃkhyātaḥ ।
1 <q>da</q> N--varṇayiṣyāmi ।
1 (rūpyanta abhinīyanta iti vā kāvyānyeva rūpāṇi ।)--Kan

vijātīyādvyāvṛttiḥ, karmalakṣaṇaṃ, prakṛṣṭaḥ ucito yogaḥ parasparasaṃbandho yathā
prakaraṇanāṭakalakṣaṇayogāt nāṭiketivṛttivibhāgastu lakṣaṇa evānupraviṣṭa iti । nāsau prayogaḥ
tathā ceti tenaiva prayogaprakāreṇānyo'pi parasparasaṃbandhavaicitryakṛto bhedaḥ utprekṣya ityarthaḥ ।
prayogāya prayogata iti vyākhyāne prayogata iti viphalameva । uktavyākhyāne tu
kohalādilakṣitatoṭakasaṭṭakarāsakādisaṅagrahaḥ phalaṃ, nāṭikāyāḥ udāharaṇatvāditi । tatroddeśaṃ
tāvadāha <q>nāṭaka</q>mityādi । saprakaraṇamiti sahaśabdenāṅkapraveśakasandhyādisāmyaṃ nāṭakena
prakaraṇasyāha । nāmnāmartho lakṣaṇa eva vyākhyāsyate । satyapi ca purāṇādāvupadeśadāyini
karmaphalasaṃbandhapradarśake tatroccāvacamaniyatakavikanthāprāyamiha tu kiñcitprayojyaṃ kiñcit
1sūcyaṃ kiñcidūhyaṃ kiñcidupekṣyamityevaṃ vaicitryayogaḥ । "sandhyādivyavasthe"ti "daśarūpaṃ
saprayojana" miti --etattu phalguprāyaṃ phalam । tatpūrvamevoktam ।
pratyakṣatoditarasāveśajanitanirvṛtisāratvādasyetihāsāderviśeṣa ityūhyam ।2

mātṛkā</q> iti ।</p>

pratītirvirasībhavet । <q>guṇai</q>rityapradhānabhūtāni ceṣṭitāni heyāni pratināyakagatāni apāya--

<lg><l>nṛpatīnāṃ yaccaritaṃ nānā1rasabhāvaceṣṭitaṃ bahudhā ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 413 !-->
pradhānāni tairyuktam । teṣāṃ pūrvapakṣasthānīyānāṃ pratikṣepeṇa siddhāntakalpasya nāyakacaritasya
nirvāhājjanapadakośādisaṃpattisamṛddhiḥ । kaumudīmahotsavādayo vilāsāḥ sandhivigrahādayo guṇā
iti vyākhyānaṃ cāṇakya(śāstra)paricayavedanamātraphalaṃ, vastuśabdena rājarṣivaṃśyacaritaśabdena ca
sarvasyārtharāśeḥ saṃgrahāt । avāntaravastusamāptau viśrāntaye ye vicchedā aṅkāḥ ye ca nimittabalāt
apratyakṣadṛṣṭānāṃ ceṣṭitānāmāvedakāḥ praveśakāḥ tairāḍhyaṃ nāṭakaṃ nāma rūpakam । tasmādasya
tannāmetyāha <q>nṛpatīnāṃ yaccarita</q>miti yadyasmānnṛpatīnāṃ saṃbandhi vyutpādyānāṃ sāmarthyāt
nṛpatīnāmeva nāṭakannāma tacceṣṭitaṃ prahvībhāvadāyakaṃ bhavati, tathā hṛdayānupraveśarañjanollāsanayā
hṛdayaṃ śarīraṃ copāyavyutpattiparighaṭṭitayā ceṣṭayā nartayati nartanṛtau1 nṛtte ityubhayathā hi
smaranti । taditi tasmāddhetoḥ, nāmāsya nāṭakamiti ।</p>
<p>nanu purāṇādyupanibaddho'pi tadarthaḥ kasmānnaṭānevedaṃ bhāvayatītyāha <q>nāneti</q> । bahuprakārā atra
saṃbhāvayanti saṃpādayanti yāni ceṣṭitāni naṭavyāpārātmāno'bhinayāḥ tairetatprahvībhāvadāyakaṃ
hṛdyatamarasāsvādasūcīdvārapraveśitaṃ tatkartavyasūtraṃ hṛdayarohaṇarūḍhaśauryādidharmaratnagrathanakāri bhavatīti
hyuktamasakṛt ।</p>
<p>nanu nṛpaticarita eva kimityayamāsvādo na devacarita ityāha <q>bahudheti</q> ।
bahuprakārāḥ upāyavaicitryādyāḥ sukhaduḥkhotpattayastāsāṃ kṛtaṃ saṃpādanaṃ yatra, devacarite

etadarthameva prakhyātagrahaṇaṃ prakarṣadyotaka punaḥ punarupāttam । ata eva vedaśāstraṃ na nāṭakaṃ, niyogena

<lg><l>1asyāvasthopetaṃ kāryaṃ 2prasamīkṣya binduvistārāt3 ।</l></lg>

<p>śrīśaṅkukastu vyācaṣṭe vijigīṣurarirmadhyamodāsīnau mitraṃ mitramitramiti । eṣāṃ caritamiti

<p>yattu kaiścidabhidhīyate--

<p>yattu paṭhitaṃ tatra dhīralalitatvaṃ rājña eva varṇanīyaṃ nānyasya, senāpatyamātyayordhīrodāttatvameva,

<p>tathā praveśakadvāreṇa mukhyacaritamapi1 śaṅkāṃ vārayitumāha ye <q>nāyakā</q> iti । dhīrodāttādayo
vijigīṣutanmitraprabhṛtayo vā ye nāyakāḥ pratināyakāśca teṣāṃ caritaṃ, tadupāyānuṣṭhānaṃ tathā <q>saṃbhogaḥ

veti <q>nāyaka</q> caritapratyakṣatayā vyutpattiḥ, prekṣakāṇāṃ <q>saṃbhogāpratyakṣatve</q> ca tadgatakevalakleśadarśanāt
vairasyaṃ sāmājikasya syāt । kimanena mahatā kaṣṭeneti tata evoktaṃ na nissukhaḥ syāditi2 ।
<q>nānāprakārāvasthau</q> pratināyakagatau caritasaṃbhogāvanupādeyāvaviṣaye ceti heyāvasthau, nāyakagatau tu
tadvaiparītyādupādeyāvasthāviti tu śabdasyārthaḥ । avikṛṣṭa ityadīrghaḥ । dīrgho hi prayoktṛprekṣakāṇāṃ
khedāya syāt ।</p>

<lg><l>1yaḥ kaścitkāryavaśādgacchati puruṣaḥ prakṛṣṭamadhvānam ।</l>
<l>tatrāpyaṅkacchedaḥ kartavyaḥ pūrvavattajjñaiḥ2 ।। 32</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 423 !-->
ityādibahu ca varṣādūrdhvamiti ca niṣedhaḥ phalguphala eva syāt । tasmādekavacanāntenaiva samāsaḥ ।
na ca rāmāyaṇabhāratādicaritatyāgaprasaṅgaḥ । kāryagrahaṇaṃ hyetadarthaṃ muninā kṛtaṃ, yatra hi yatnaniṣpādyaṃ
sañcitaṃ tadeva varṣaṃ gaṇyate varṣāntarāṇi tu tatra vidyamānānyapi avidyamānakalpāni । rāmacarite
hi caturdaśavarṣāṇyaraṇyanivāso yadyapi kāryaḥ, varṣāṇi1 tricaturāṇi bhavanti yatra
mārīcavadhasugrīvarājyadānādyavāntarakāryaṃ saṃbhavati । tasmādvarṣādūrdhvamityanena kāryaṃ varṣadvayādi
niṣidhyata ityevaṃ varṣasahasrāyuṣo'pi varṣaśatāntarālavṛttacaritavyākhyāne'pi na kiñcidduṣyati ।
tena pañcāṅke nāṭake pañca kāryadinānīti saṃkṣepaḥ, daśāṅke tu daśeti vistaraḥ ।</p>
<p>aṅkacchede nimittāntaramapyāha--<q>yaḥ kaścitkāryavaśādi</q>ti । kāryavaśātkāryasya
tatrāyatatvāt yaḥ puruṣo nāyakaḥ so'nekayojanavyavahitamadhvānaṃ yadā2 pratidinaṃ gamanaṃ viśrāntiḥ
śayyetyevamādi kathaṃ raṅge pradarśya3 tadantenāṅkacchedaḥ kāryaḥ । ḍimādināyakasya tu
divyasyākāśayānakādinā sarvaṃ yujyate । anāyaka puruṣastvavicchinna evāṅke niṣkrāmati । nanu
divasāvasānakāryaṃ kenopapadyata iti <q>āvaśyakāvirodhene</q>tyādinā yaduktaṃ tatastilamātreṇāpyadhikaṃ
vācyamasya na labhyate vākyasya । ata evaitat <q>bhaṭṭalollaṭādyairna</q> paṭhitameva ।।</p>
<p>upādhyāyāstvāhuḥ--nedaṃ nimittāntaraṃ api tu pūrvaṃ tāvatkathitaṃ <q>yadyaṅke nopapadyata</q> iti
tasyaivodāharaṇamanayaivāryayā darśitam । yathā nāyakasya prakṛṣṭādhvagamanamiti pūrvavaditi tadarhamiti4
bhavati pūrvalakṣaṇārho'ṅkacchedo'yamiti yāvat । apiśabda udāharaṇāntaramapi sūcayati ।
aṅkārthasandhānaprayojanasya praveśakasya sthānaṃ vācyam । viṣayaṃ cāha aṅkāntarānusārīti aṅkamadhye
bhavatīti yāvat । aṅkāntaraṃ pūrvāṅkāntaramanusarati tasya paścādbhavatītyarthaḥ । pratyaṅkāntaṃ yo binduḥ
anusandhānābhidhāyivākyaṃ5 yatsaṃkṣiptaṃ prayojanaṃ tadadhikatākaraṇaṃ vistāramuddiśyeti vācyamuktaṃ,

<p>tadayamatrārthaḥ --yatra dicasakāryāṇyayanekāni tatra tanmadhye1 yatsundaraprayogamupadeśopayogi ca
tatpratyakṣeṇa darśanīyam । anyatsarvaṃ praveśakena vṛttāntārthā tadavaśiṣṭenetivṛttanirvāhaphalā alpā

darśayati <q>yuddhaṃ rājyabhraṃśa</q> ityādi । yuddhe śastrasaṃpātasya bāhulyaṃ rājyabhraṃśe'pi patanamaraṇādeḥ
nagaroparodhe balasya yantrasuruṅgādidānasya [ca] । iha kecidāhuḥ maraṇaṃ dvividham, kiñcidanyasaṃbandhinyā
kriyayā saṃpādyaṃ yathā cakreṇa daityasya śiraśchedaṃ,1 kiñcidanyasaṃbandhikriyānairapekṣyeṇaiva
vyādhyabhighātādiprabhavam, tatrādyasyaiva niṣedhaḥ kriyate । etadarthameva kṛtagrahaṇaṃ, taddhyanyakriyāvācakaṃ
na ca tadyuddhena saṃgṛhītam, ayuddhe pūrvakasyāpyaśaṅkitaśiraśchedasya darśitatvāditi । ta evaṃ
praṣṭavyāḥ-- idaṃ maraṇaṃ prayojyamidaprayojyamiti na tāvadatra viṣayavibhāge nidānamutpaśyāmaḥ ।
mṛtasya kathaṃ niṣkrāmaṇaṃ kathaṃ vāvasthānaṃ, tato nāṭyopayogisamastadhruvāgānādiprakriyāvilopaḥ
sāmājikānāṃ virasatāpratipattiriti tu sarvatra maraṇaṃ samānaṃ tasmādraṅge maraṇamaprayojyameva । nanu
maraṇānubhāvavarṇanenedānīṃ kiṃ kṛtyaṃ, yuddhavīraraudrādāvapyetadanubhāvavarṇane kiṃ prayojanaṃ tadanubhāvāparijñāne
praveśakairapi kathaṃ varṇanaṃ syāditi cenmaraṇe'pi samaḥ samādhiḥ ।</p>

mūlaṃ parapuruṣasaṃbhāvanāmūlatvāt । evamanabhyupagame tu śvaśureṇa vadhvā asannihite putre nirvāsanaṃ
śabarasenāpatigṛhe'vasthānamityuttamaprakṛtīnāmanupapannameva । tasmāt svavargāpekṣayedamuttamatvamadyatane
rājocitānāmuttamaprakṛtīnāṃ vaṇiṅmātre samāropya taddūṣaṇaṃ yatkṛtaṃ na tena brahmayaśaḥsvāmiyaśaḥ

eva nāyakaḥ kevalamanyavaṇigapekṣayā sa uttamo'stu, vyutpādyaśca tatraivaṃvidha evetyalamavāntareṇa ।</p>

<p>nanu kohalena mukhāṅkasya cāyamantarāntare vihitaḥ
<lg><l>"madhyamapuruṣaniyojyo nāṭakamukhasandhimātrasañcāraḥ ।</l>

tatkathamuktamaṅkāntarānusārīti, upalakṣaṇārthametadityadoṣaḥ । tathāhi bījaṃ binduśca prathamamupakṣipyete,

vā yatra mantracintāyāmanupraveśyate tatra praveśako'pi prathamopakṣepe na yogya1 iti yuktam ।
sāmānyenāṅkāntarānusārīti aṅkasya madhya ityanena prastāvanāṅkamadhyavartitāpyuktaiva ।
praveśakaviṣkambhakaviṣaye liṅgavacanayoratantratvāt strīṇāmapyanupraveśaḥ saṃkhyādhikyasya ca ।</p>
<p>evaṃ sakalapuruṣārthaviṣayā vyutpattiḥ nāṭakena pradhānasya rājaprāyasya kriyate,
prakaraṇena ca madhyamaprāyasya, apūrvakutūhalavatastatrāpi caikaviṃśakasyābhidhānāt

yatra śūnye tena varṇyante vā kaścitpaśyatyākarṇayati ca tatra ca tadvacanaṃ sa evānuvadan
sāmājikān bodhayati । yathā "bho bāḍaba, ale kiṃ bravīṣi" ityādau na kevalaṃ paravacanamabhinayet,
kintu prativacanaiḥ svoktaiḥ saha, ata<q>evottarottaragrathitaiḥ</q> yojanābhirupalakṣitaiḥ । nanu yo'sāveko'tra
praviśati sa ka ityāha <q>dhūrtaviṭeti</q> । nānāprakārāvasthāviśeṣāt lokopayogivyavahārātmakātmā2
vācyaṃ yasya, ata eva <q>bahuceṣṭaḥ satataṃ kārya</q> iti sakalasāmānyapṛthaggatopayogyastu3 lokavyavahāro
veśyāviṭādivṛttāntātmā nirūpyata iti bāhulyena pṛthagjanavyutpattiyoni4rūpakamidaṃ rājaputrādīnāmapi
śaṃbhalīvṛttānto jñeya evāvañcanārthamiti <q>saṃprayojya</q>5 ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>idamiha mīmāṃsyaṃ--ya ete utsṛṣṭikādayo6 rūpakabhedāḥ te tāvadekarasā eva, yadyapi
nāṭakādayo'pyevameva । tathāhi7 sarvarasayogyatāyāmapi nāṭake prakaraṇe ca dharmārthādivīra eva

pradhānaṃ paramārthataḥ sarveṣu nāyakabhedeṣu vīratvānugamadarśanāt । samavakāre tu yadyapi hi śrṛṅgārāditvamuktaṃ
tathāpi vīra eva pradhānaṃ raudro vā, ḍimavyāyogayorapyevam । īhāmṛge'pi raudraprādhānyameva,
nāṭikāyāṃ tu śrṛṅgāra eva pradhānam । evaṃ tāvad vīraraudraśrṛṅgārā yathāsvaṃ [kiṃ] pumarthatrayaprāṇabhūtatvena
vartamānā, eteṣu prayogeṣu śāntabībhatsarasau tu caramapumarthayogāttatra ca sarvasya nādhikāro'pi
kasyācidapaścimajanmano'dhikārānnāṭake yadyapi tatphalapradhānatayā prādhānyamavalambeyātāṃ tathāpi
nāsau pracuraprayoga iti tayoḥ puruṣārthapravaraprāṇitayorapi vīrādirasāntarādhyāvāpenāvasthāpanam ।
evaṃ tāvatpumarthaviṣayo rūpakarasaviṣaya eva paramārthataḥ, tathāpi tvitivṛttavaitatyādrasāntaraprayogo'pi
tadaṅgatayā tatra bhavati । evaṃ tatpradhānaceṣṭāyogāddhṛttivaicitryamatrocitameva । utsṛṣṭikāṅkaprahasanabhāṇāstu
karuṇahāsyavismayapradhānatvād rañjakarasapradhānāḥ, tata evātra strībālamūrkhādiradhikārī । na ca
vitatamatretivṛttam, itivṛttavaicitryamapi tatra nāsti । tathāhi--utsṛṣṭikāṅke tu vṛttitrayaṃ tāvadvacasā
niṣiddhaṃ, bhāratī cātra kathaṃ vṛttiḥ, ceṣṭā hi karuṇe'pradhānaṃ, tadupakaraṇaṃ tu paridevitātmikā
bhāratī, tasmāt phalasaṃvittyākhyā vṛttiḥ, vākceṣṭayoḥ phalānubhava iti yasyā lakṣaṇaṃ, sābhyupagantavyā ।
avaśyaṃ caitat, anyathā mūrchāmaraṇādau vākceṣṭayorabhāve nirvṛttikataiva syāt । kiñca yadi
tāvatpumarthakāmoddeśena kaiśikyabhidhīyate dharmamarthaṃ coddiśya vṛttidvayaṃ vaktavyam । tasmācceṣṭātmikā
nyāyavṛttiranyāyavṛttirvāgrūpā tatphalabhūtā phalasaṃvittiriti vṛttitrayameva yuktāmiti <q>bhaṭṭodbhaṭo</q>
manyate ।</p>
<p>yadāha--

layatālagānāni pravartante, saṃvedanamapi ca mūrchādau nāstīti śakyaṃ vaktumiti phalavṛtti--

<p><q>ākṣipte</q> tviti । <q>śubhā</q>śubhaṃ daivaṃ tenābuddhipūrvakaṃ kutracidarthe <q>ākṣipte'pi</q>
kauśalāttattatpracchādanecchayā yatrotta<q>ro1'nyo'rtha</q> ucyate <q>tadavaspa</q>nditaṃ cakṣuḥ--
spandanādivadantargatasūcanīyasaṃbhavāt । yathā--
<lg><l>satpakṣā madhuragiraḥ prasādhitāśā madoddhatārambhāḥ ।</l>
<l>nipatanti dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kālavaśānmedinīpṛṣṭhe ।। (veṇī 1/6)</l></lg>
atra daivavaśādayamartha āyātaḥ satpakṣe amadhurāgīryeṣānte, tathā prakarṣeṇa sādhitāḥ ādhisahitāḥ
yairdiśaḥ kṛtāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajāḥ patantīti । tatrottaraṃ pratihatamamaṅgalam । punaḥ sūtradhāraḥ nanu
śaratsamayavarṇanayā haṃsā nabhastalaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā iti vyapadiśāmītyādi avaspanditatvameva sūcayati
"na khalu na jāne kintvamaṅgalatvāt śaṅkitameva me hṛdaya" miti ।</p>
<p><q>hāsyenopagatārtheti</q> prahelikā paravi2tāraṇakāri yaduttaraṃ, ata eva hāsyayuktā sā nālikā
praṇālikā vyājetyarthaḥ । prakarṣeṇa helikā narmādikrīḍārūpaṃ yasyāḥ sā prahelikā । yathā--
susaṃgatā "jasya kide tumaṃ āadā so ettha evva ciṭhṭhadi ।" <q>sāgarikā</q> "sahi kassa
kide" । susaṅgatā (sahāsam) "ai appasaṅkīdeṇaṃ cittaphalaassa" । anayā bhaṅgyā ācchāditaṃ
